|| nachAMshimArgasyeti || aMshini j~nAnini sukhini duHkhini chAMshe j~nAnAdyabhAvenAMshimArgasyAMshenAgamyatvAdityarthaH | aMshAMshinorbhedAbhAve, j~nAnAdibhedo na syAditi bhAvaH | nachAMshinorbhinnatvenAMshino.anAditvepyaMshasyAtpattisambhavAdindrAdijIvAMshAnAmarjunAdInAmevotpattimatvena, taddharmabhUtayogyatAyA anAditvAsambhavAnna tatsApekShatvamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "vyatirekastadbhAvabhAvitvAnna tUpalabdhivat.h' ityatra, tajj~nAnAdibhede vidyamAne.api, aMshAMshinorbhedaM nirAkurvatA j~nAnAdibhedAdaMshasyAMshimArgagantR^itvAditi sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena, "sAdhanottamatA' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- sAdhanottamasyeti || aMshaH, aMshino bhinno na bhavati, tadgatasukhaduHkhAdyanusandhAtR^itvAt.h | yo yadgatasukhaduHkhAdyanusandhAtAH sa tadabhinnaH | yathA sampratipanna iti prayogo.atrAbhipretaH | nanvaMshasyAMshigatasukhaduHkhAdyanusandhAnamevAsiddham.h | tathAtve.arjunAderindrAdyabhimatakhANDavadAhAdau pravR^ittyabhAvApatterityata ukttam.h- uttameti || yadyapyaMshakR^itAlpasAdhanajanyaphale j~nAnAdAvaMshino.anusandhAnaM nAsti, tathApi pradhAnopAsanAdiphalAnusandhAnamastyeva | aMshagataj~nAnAderaMshinAnubhUyamAnatvAt.h | aMshigatasarvAnanusandhAnasyeshvarAchintyashaktayAyattatvAt.h | tathAcha nAsmAbhiraMshigatAsheShasukhAdyanusandhAtR^itvaM hetUkR^itam.h | yenAsiddhaH | kiM tvananusandhAnamAtram.h | tachchAstIti bhAvaH | nanvaMshasyAMshigatasukhAdyanusandhAtR^itve.api tayorbheda evAstu, vipakShe bAdhakAbhAvAt.h | ityatra Aha- 
anyathAdR^iShyaM vinA sharIrAnupapatteH || 35 || 
|| anyatheti || aMshAMshinorbhedeM.ashAnAM sharIreNa sahotpattau tachCharIrajanakAdR^iShyasya pUrvamAshrayAbhAve.adR^iShyAkhyakAraNaM vinA sharIrendriyAdyutpattyanupapatterityarthaH | atrAMshimArgasyAMshena gamyatvaM sarvathA chedasiddham.h | ekadeshena chedanyathAsiddhamiti bhAvaH | evaMcha sAdhanottamasyAMshenAnubhUyamAnatvAt.h,. aMshAMshinorabheda eveti yukttopAsanAdAvanAdAvanAdiyogyatApekSheti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH, "AtmanaH sharIram.h' ityanenAMshikakarmanirmitasharIre vidyamAnatvAdityarthakena sUchitaH |) || 35 || OM aN^gAvabaddhAstu na shAkhAsu hi prativedaM OM || ityatra, brahmopAsanavidheraN^gadevatopAsanasAhityAsAhityasAdhAraNyAdbhagavadupAsanamaN^gadevatopAsanAyukttaM vA kartavyamuta kevalaM veti sandehe, kevalamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, aN^gadevatopAsanAyukttamiti siddhAntaH | tatrApi bhagavadupAsanasyAN^gadevatAsAhityena kartavyatve, upAsanasya guNopasaMhArapUrvakatvAllaukikapuuruShapUjAdau dvaividhyadarshanena, kimekasya shrutipratipAditA guNAH sarveShUpasaMhartavyA na veti sandehe, upasaMhartavyA iti pUrvaH pakShaH, neti siddhAntaH | tatra, "sandhAnam.h' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha guNAntarasandhAnasya kvApi darshanamAtreNa samAdhikAN^gadevatAntaraguNA apyaN^gadevatAntare upasaMhartavyA | nAnAguNatvena teShAM shrutidR^iShyeH | aniShiddhaguNAnAM vAkyAnvayanyAyenopasaMhArAt.h na shAkhAsvityAdivisheShaH | uttameShvadhamaguNApekShayA mantrAdivadveti || 36 || 
|| nacha guNAntareti || atha guNAnAmuttameShUpasaMhArasya siddhAnte.apyaN^gIkArAtsamAdhiketyukttam.h | ayamarthaH |  yadyaN^gadevatAsAhityena brahmopAsanaM kartavyam.h tarhi upAsanAyA guNopasaMhArapUrvakatvAdguNAntarANAM devatvAdInAM sandhAnasyAnusandhAnasyopasaMhArasya savareShu deveShu darshanamAtreNa samAdhikAN^gadevatAntarANAM sUryAdyaN^gadevatAbhyo bhinnAnAM brahmarudrAdInAM ye guNAH sUryAdyayogyAste.apyaN^gadevatAntare sUryAdAvupasaMhartavyAH syuH | na chaivam.h | tasmAdbAdhakopetAttamevaikaM jAnatha AtmAnamanyathA vAcho vimuJNchatha, pUjayennAnyA devatA ityAderanyadevatopAsananiShedhAtkevalameva brahmopAsanaM kartavyamiti | evaMcha devatAntaraguNasya devatAntare.anusandhAnaprAptyAN^gadevAnAmanupAsyatvAttadabhidhAyakavedavaiyarthyamiti neti bhAvaH | ayaM cha nyAyo "mantrAdivadvA' ityanena, adhamaguNAnAmuttama upasaMhAroktayA, kasyachidguNasyAnusandhAne sarveShAmeva guNAnAmanusandhAnaM na syAditi sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "nAnAdR^iShyiH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- nAnAguNatveneti || parasparavilakShaNaguNatvena teShAmaN^gadevatAnAM shrutiShu dR^iShyerityarthaH | tatashcha sUryAdyasambhAvitaguNavattvena brahmarudrAdInAM uttamatvAduttamasambandhiguNAnAM chAdhameShu ayogyatvAdbrahmAdyaN^gadevatAguNajAtaM sUryAdiShu nopasaMhAryaM, kintu yogyameveti bhAvaH | nanu "na shAkhAsu hi prativedam.h' iti vedapratItaguNAnAM upasaMhArAbhAvamabhidhAya, "mantrAdivadvA' iti kathaM tadviruddha upasaMhAro.abhidhIyate, ityAshaN^kAparihArArthaM 
tayorviShayabhedamAha- aniShiddheti || brahmarudrAdiguNAnAM sUryAdAvayogyatve.api, tatrAniShiddhAnAM yogyAnAM guNAnAM vAkyAnvayanyAyena yathA khalu bhagavatpratipAdaka "sahasrashIrShA puruShaH' ityAdivAkyAnAM sarveShAmanyatra chaturmukhAdau sambandhAbhAve.api, "hiraNyagarbhaH samavatartAgre' ityAdInAM tadyogyAnAM sambandhastathetyanena nyAyenopasaMhArAddhetoH, na shAkhAsvityAdau Adipadena prativedamiti sUtrasheShasya, "samatvAdvA' itismR^iteshcha grahaNam.h | visheShaH ayogyaguNopasaMhArarUpavisheShaH, niShedhaviShaya ityarthaH | "R^ite tatra prasiddhAshcha' ityR^igbhAShyopapAditaprakAreNa yathAgnyAdyadhamadevatAviShayamantravidyAdikaM brahmAdyuttamadevatAviShayatvenAdhIyate, uttamAnAM tatpratipAdyatvAt.h | evamuttameShu brahmAdiShvadhamAnAM rudrAdInAM guNAnAmupasaMhAre na kashchiddoSha ityadhamaguNApekShayA "mantrAdivadvA' iti sUtrapravR^ittirityarthaH | evaMcha nyAyadR^iShyayA yathAyogyamevAN^gadevatopAsanaM kartavyamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH, "samatvAt.h' itisUchitasUchakena hishabdena sUchitaH |) || 36 || OM bhUmnaH kratuvajjyAyastvaM tathA cha darshayati OM || ityatra, sarvopAsyasarvAnupAsyaguNadarshanAdbhagavatsambandhI bhUmaguNaH sarvopAsye na veti sandehe, neti pUrvaH pakShaH, sarvopAsya iti siddhAntaH | tatra, "iShyaM phalam.h' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha bhUmagurasyopAsakaM prati visheShAbhAve.api tattadiShyaguNAnusAreNa phalopapattirityavisheShaH | 
|| nacha bhUmaguNasyeti || upAsakaM prati bhUmaguNasya sambhR^ityAdibhyo.anupAsyatvena visheShAbhAve.api tasya upAsakasya iShyA apekShitA, ye AnandAdayo guNAH tadanusAreNa tadupAsanAnusAreNa phalasya iShyasyAnandAderupapattirityato hetoH priyashirastvAdiguNavadAnandAdivisheShaNatve.api bhUmaguNasyAnupAsyatvena priyashirastvAdyavisheSha ityarthaH | anenAnuvyAkhyAne "iShyam.h' ityetat.h "saptasu prathamA' iti sUtrAttR^itIyAntatvena prathamAntatvena cha tantreNopAttamiti vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | evaMcheShyenopAsitena viShNvAnandAdineShyaM jIvasyAvirbhUtAnandAdirUpaM kathamupapadyata iti, iShyaphalasyAnyathAsiddherbhUmatvamanupAsyamiti nAlaukikatayopAsanamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo "jyAyastvam.h' ityanena dR^iShTAnAmAnandAdiguNAnAM bhUmatvena sahopAsane, etatphalaM bhavati, nAnyatheti bhUmasya jyAyastvaM vadatA bhUmatvaM vinAnaitenopAsitena guNena phalamiti sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena, "shiShyiH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM shrutyudAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- 
bhUmaiva devaH paramo hyupAsyA naivAbhUmA phalameShAM vidhatta ityAdishiShyeH || 37 || 
|| bhUmaiva deva iti || tasmAdbhUmA guNato vai vishiShyo yathA kratuH karmamadhye vishiShyaH' iti sheShaH | shrutiyojanA tu hi yasmAt.h paramo devo bhUmA bhUmatvenAnupAsitaH eShAmupAsakAnAM phalaM naiva vidhatte | tasmAdyathA kratuH karmamadhye vishiShyaH, tathA bhUmaguNo guNarAshito vishiShyaH | tato bhUmatvenaivopAsya iti shiShyeH shAsanAt.h upAsyA iti vidheriti yAvat.h | atra pUvarpakShahetorasiddhirabhipretA | evaMcha bhUmatvAnupAsane phalAbhAvena, phalArthaM bhUmaiva deva iti bhUmatvopAsanashiShyeH na bhUmatvasya sambhR^ityAdyavisheShaH | kintu bhUmatvaM sarvairupAsyamiti na laukikatayopAsanamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "tathA hi darshayati' ityanenokttaH |) || 37 || OM nAnAshabdAdibhedAt.h OM || ityatra, ekAnekaprakAratayAdR^ishyamAnavastupratItyA, bhUmaguNaH kimadhikAriNAM tAratamyena pratIyate, utaikaprakAreNeti sandehe, ekaprakAreNeti pUrvaH pakShaH, tAratamyeneti siddhAntaH | tatra, "akalpanA' ityuktapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradasharnapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha bhUmaguNa upAsakAnAmekaprakAreNaiva pratIyata ityaN^gIkAyarm.h | 
|| nacha bhUmaguNa iti || upAsakAnAmityuktayA, pratIyate ityatropAsane iti lakShyate | kuta ityata Aha-  
visheShasyakalpanopapatteriti na mantavyam.h yAvAnevAdhikAreShu visheSho.anUna eva hi tato bhUmatvadR^iShyau cha brahmAdInAM pR^ithakpR^ithak.h iti visheShasyAnUnatvavachanAt.h || 38 || 
||visheShasyeti || visheShakalpanAnupapatterityarthaH | keShAJNchitsamyakpUrNAnanda iti keShAJNchitkiJNchitpUrNAnanda ityupAsanasya mithyopAsanatvenAyogAdityarthaH | evaMcha bhUmatve visheShasyAkalpanAdbhUmatvamekaprakAreNaiva pratIyata iti nokttatAratamyaM yukttamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH, nAnetyanena bhUmatvasya nAnAprakAratvAktayA asambhavenAvisheShakalpanAditi sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "anunatA' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM pramANodAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- yAvAniti || brahmAdInAmupAsanAdhikAreShu yAvAneva visheShaH tAratamyarUpaH | tato visheShAdanUna eva visheShaH bhUmatvAvAntaravisheShaH, bhUmatvadR^iShyau brahmAdInAM pR^ithakpR^ithageva pratIyate | yadvA, tasmAn.h brahmAdInAmadhikAreShu visheShastAratamyarUpo.anUna eva, tato hetoryAvAneva bhUmaguNo visheSho bhUmatvadR^iShyayA viShayIkartuM yogyastAvanpR^ithakpR^ithageva brahmAdInAM pratIyata iti yojanA | visheShasya 
upAsyAnandAdiguNavisheShaNIbhUtabhUmatvavisheShasya, brahmAdyadhikArivisheShApekShayAnUnatvasyAnusAritvavachanAdityarthaH | anena pUrvapakShahetorasiddhirukttA bhavati | nacha, bhUmatve visheShAnupapatteH, kathamasiddhiriti vAchyam.h, atItavatsarANAM mAsAnAM chAnantye.api visheShavadbhUmatve.api visheShopapatteH | rudrAdibhirbhUmatvopAsane chatadurmukhAdiyogyabhUmatvaniShedhAnnAnyathopAsanamapIti bhAvaH | evaMcha bhUmatvavisheShasyAdhikArAdanUnatayAdhikAriNAM yukttaM tAratamyamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH, "shabdAdibhedAt.h' ityanena "yAvAnevAdhikAreShu' ityAdipramANAnusAreNa pratIyata iti sUchitaH |) || 38 || vikalpo vishiShyaphalatvAt.h OM || ityatra, bimbopAsteranavadhAraNAt.h  bhagavadupAsanasya svabimbAtirikttarUpaviShayatve svabimbamAtraviShayatve vopapannatayA bhagavadupAsanaM mumukShUNAM svabimbAtirikttarUpaviShayaM kartavyaM, na veti sandehe, neti pUrvaH pakShaH, svamokShasAdhanAtirikttaM narasiMhAdyupAsanaM kartavyameveti siddhAntaH | tatra, "shuddhavairUpyam.h' ityakttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUvarkaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha shuddhamokShasAdhanavairUpyAnmokShasAdhanatvenopadiShyaM vinA viShNAvevopAsanAntarasyAkartavyatA avighnatAsAdhanatvAt.h || 3 9 || 
|| nacha shuddheti || shuddhasya niShkAmasya mokShasAdhanabimbopAsanasya, vairUpyAt.h vighnakaratvena viruddhatvAt.h, mokShasAdhanopadiShyaM bimbopAsanaM vinA, viShNau viShNuviShaya eva, evakAreNa kartavyatvena priAptaM sUchayati | upAsanAntarasya bimbAtirikttarUpopAsanasyetyarthaH | evaMcha bimbAtirikttopAsanasya shuddhavairUpyAdakartavyatvena tadabhidhAyakavedavaiyarthyamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo "vikalpaH' ityanena vighnAdibhave kartavyam.h, tadabhAve na kartavyamiti vighnAlpoktyA  kartavyatAniyame bimbopAsanavilambahetutvena shuddhavairUpyamiti sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "avighnatvam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- avighneti || na vidyate vighno yasya, tasya bhAvo.avighnAtA, vishiShyamokShasyeti sheShaH | tatashcha mokShasAdhanabimbopAsanAnantaraM kriyamANasya bimbAtirikttanarasiMhAdyupAsanasya vishiShyamokShapratibandhakaduritanivartakatvena vishiShyamokShasyAvighnatAsAdhantavAchChuddhavairUpyaM tasyAsiddhamiti bhAvaH | evaMchAvighnatAhetutvena bimbAtirikttamapyupAsyamiti na tadvidyAvaiyarthyamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "vishiShyaphalatvAt.h' ityanena nR^isiMhAdyupAsanasya bimbopAsanAnantarabhAvitvena duritAdinivR^ittilakShaNamokShopayogiphalasAdhanatvamiti sUchitaH |) OM kAmyAstu yathAkAmaM samuchchIyeranna vA pUrvahetvabhAvAt.h OM || ityatra, AvashyakavaikalpikopAsanapratItyA, kAmasAdhanabhagavadrUpaguNaviShayamupAsanaM kimAvashyakaM vaikalpikaM veti sandehe, Avashyakamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, vaikalpikamiti siddhAntaH | tatra, "aN^gatvam.h' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha kAmyasAdhanAnamapi guNAnAmaN^gatvAdevopasaMhArakartavyatAniyamaH | anupasaMhAre virodhAbhAvAt.h | kAmyAnAmaniyatAN^gatvAchcha | arthAdidharmasiddhau hi na niyatyAN^gamiShyata iti brahmatarke || 40 || 
|| nacha kAmyasAdhanAnAmiti || AdipadaM nR^isiMhatvAdisamuchchayArtham.h |  bimbaguNasamuchchayAtharM vA | aN^gatvAnmokShasAdhanaj~nAnasAdhanArthAdiphalopAsanaviShayatvena mokShopayogitvAt.h | evakAreNa tadupAsanasyAvashyakatvaM sUchayati | siddhAntavaiShamyapradarshanArthaM-  niyama ityukttam.h | evaMcha kAmyopAsanasya mokShAN^gatvenAvashyakatvAdvayarthaH prathamapAda iti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "hetvabhAvAt.h' ityanena, arthasya j~nAnAN^gakatvagrAhakAnvayavyatirekarUpahetvabhAvAditi vadatA sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena, "avirodhaH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- anupasaMhAra iti || svabimbopAsanenaiva j~nAnasiddhau, j~nAnAsiddhirUpavirodhasya nR^isiMhAdyupAsana iva vishiShyamokShapratibandhakaduritanivR^ittyabhAvarUpavirodhasya chAbhAvAdityarthaH | sAdhakAbhAvAchcha na niyama ityAha- kAmyAnAmiti || j~nAnaM pratyarthAdInAmaniyatAN^gatvAdityarthaH | arthAdikaM vinApi j~nAnotpatteH kvachidarthe satyapi j~nAnAnutpatteranvayavyatirekavyabhichArAditi bhAvaH | atra pramANamAha- arthAdIti || dharmapadena j~nAnamapyupalakShyate | kvachidarthAdinA dharmAsiddheH niyamyetyukttam.h | evaMcha kAmyaguNAnAmanupasaMhAre virodhAbhAvAt.h kAmyopAsanasyavaikalpikatvAt.h, sArthakyaM vairAgyapAdasyeti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo "hetvabhAvAt.h' ityAdinaiva virodhaphalahetvabhAvAditi vadatA sUchitaH |) || 40 || aN^geShu hathAshrayabhAvaH OM || ityatra, bhagavadaN^gAshritatvena shrutivachanasya tathopAsane.anupAsane.api sambhavAt.h, brahmAdInAM bhagavadaN^gAshritatvenopAsanaM mumukShuNA kartavyaM na veti sandehe, na kartavyamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, katarvyamiti siddhAntaH | tatra, "avisheShadR^ishiH' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati-
nacha devAdInAmiti tatraiva visheShavachanAbhAvAdbrahmA shirasi lalATe rudra ityAdInAM nAvashyopAsyatA devAdInAmeva | 
|| nacha devAdInAmiti || devAdInAmeveti kartari ShaShThI | "AnandAdayaH pradhAnasya' iti siddhAnte manuShyANAM chaturguNavyatirikttaguNopAsanAniShedhAt.h, devAnAmiti vishiShyokttam.h | tatraivaM brahmA shirasi lalATe rudra ityAdivAkyokttabrahmAshrayashIrShatvAdInAM devAdibhireva nAvashyopAsyeti bhAvaH | evaMcha bhagavadaN^gAshritadevopAsanaM devaiH kartavyamiti visheShavachanAbhAvAditareShAM tatrAdhikArAbhAvAnniradhikArikameva prAptamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "samAhArAchcha' ityanena "dhyAyet.h' iti shrutisUchakena vishiShyaguNarUpaphalAnusAreNa devAnAmevAdhikArasiddherityarthakenAN^gadevatopAsane devAnAmiti visheShato.adhikArasyAnukttatvAditi sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "guNavaisheShyam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM shrutyudAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- 
dhyAyedaN^geShvaN^gadevatAH parasya vishiShyA hi guNAmukttau devAnAM bhavanti te hi tAdR^ishAste hi hareranurUpA iti shruterguNavaisheShyAt.h || 41 ||
|| dhyAyediti || aN^gadevatAH paramasyAN^geShu tattadaN^gotpannatvena tattadAshritatvena dhyAyet.h | etaddhayAnaM devAnAmeva kuta ityata ukttam.h- vishiShyA hIti || hi yasmAt.h, devAnAmeva mukttau vishiShyA guNAH paramasthAnaprabhR^itayo bhavanti | tarhi phalArthibhiH sarvairetadupAsanasya kartavyatve devAnAmeveti kathamityata ukttam.h- te hIti || hi yasmAt.h, te devAH, tAdR^ishAH ukttaphalayogyAH, tadapi kuta ityata ukttam.h- te hi hareriti || guNavaisheShyAt.h devAdInAmevetyatrApi sambaddhayate | tenottarAdhikaraNasya devavyatirikttaviShayatvasUchanena virodhaparihAro.api sUchitaH | tatashcha haryanurUpatvaparamasthAnaprAptilakShaNaphalayogyatvAdiguNAnAM devAnAmeva vaisheShyAtteShAmevokttopAsanAyAmadhikAra ityarthaH | evaMcha devAnAM guNavaisheShyAtteShAmevAN^gadevatopAsane.adhikAra iti sArthakyaM tadvidyAnAmiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "samAhArAt.h' ityanenaiva sUchitaH | ) || 41 || OM na vA tatsahabhAvAchChruteH  OM || ityatra, kartavyAkartavyopAsanapratItyA bhagavadaN^gAshritatvenopAsanaM kartavyaM na veti sandehe, neti pUrvaH pakShaH, devaireva kartavyamiti siddhAntaH | tatra, "kriyA' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM sAkShAtpUrvapakShasAdhakasUchanAya tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- 
nacha kriyAtvAdupAsanAyAH agniShyomAdivatpratishAkhaM vakttavyatA | upAsanAyajanaM cheti sAmyaM tattadvisheShAnsaMharetsarvatashcha | tathA kartR^iNAM tatphalAnAM visheShAdvayarthA hi shAkhA anyathaivaM cha sArthA ityupAsanAvisheShANAM tvadhikArivisheShANAM chAgame.avagamAt.h || 42 || 
|| iti shrImannyAyavivaraNe tR^itIyAdhyAyasya tR^itIyaH pAdaH || 
|| nacha kriyAtvAditi || aN^gadevatopAsanAyAH kartavyatve, kriyAtvAdagniShyomAdivatpratishAkhaM sarvashAkhAsu vakttavyatA syAditi sheShaH | na chaivam.h | tasmAtpratishAkhamanuktteH nAN^gadevatopAsanaM kairapi katarvyamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH sarvashAkAgatopAsanasahapAThAbhAvena vyavasthitavikalpaM samarthayatA sUtreNa sarvopAsyatve kriyAtvAtsarvairavashyakartavyatvAtsarvatra vakttavyatA syAditi sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "AgamaH' ityakttasiddhAntanyAyaM shrutyudAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- upAsanenati || yadyapyupAsanA yajanaM chetyanayoH kriyAtvena sAmyam.h, tathApi tadvisheShAchchaturmukhAshrayashIrShatvAdibhagavaddharmavisheShAt.h sarvataH pratipAdakashAkhAbhyaH saMharet.h | upasaMhR^ityopAsIta cha | kuta ityata ukttam.h- tathA kartR^iNAmiti || vikShipya tatrokttAnAM chaturmukhAshrayashIrShatvAdibhagavadguNAnAM upasaMhR^ityopAsanAkartR^iNAM tatphalAnAM teShAM tadupAsanaphalAnAM visheShatkartR^iNAM karaNameva kiM na syAdityata ukttam.h- vyarthA hIti || hi yasmAt.h, anyathA aN^gAshritatvena devatopAsanasya sarvathA kartavyatve shAkhAH "brahmA shirasi lalATe rudraH' ityiAdakA vyatharAH | evaMcha devaiH kartavyatve tadupAsanasya, "shAkhAH sArthAH saprayojanAH' ityAdyAgamanepAsanAvisheShANAM tatratatrokttachaturmukhAshrayashIrShatvAdiguNopasaMhArapUrvakaM kR^itopAsanAnAmadhikarivisheShANAM devAdInAM chashabdAtphalavisheShANAM chAvagamAdityarthaH | adhikArivisheShANAmiti vadatA pratishAkhamanuktternimittAntaraM sUchitaM sarvaiH kartavyamiti | anena pUrvapakShahetoranyathAsiddhirapi j~nApitA | evaMchAgamenAN^gadevatopAsanasya devaireva kartavyatAvagamAdyukttaM tadvidyAnAM sArthakyaM, iti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo "darshanAchcha' ityanenokttaH |) || 42 || 
|| iti shrImannyAyavivaraNabhAvabodhe tR^itIyAdhyAyasya tR^itIyaH pAdaH || 
upAsanAnitabhagavadaparokShaj~nAnasAmarthyapratipAdanArthamayaM pAdaH pravR^ittaH | etatpAdAntargatAdhikaraNapUrvapakShasiddhAntanyAyA anuvyAkhyAyAM saN^graheNokttAH | "audAryamuchchAvachashakttirAtmasvarUpadArDhyaM cha nijasvabhAvaH | svAtantyamApUrNavisheShayogyatA virodhahAnishcha chaturthapAde | vyavasthitisvavisheShasthitishcha niShedhasAmAnyavividhikriyANAm.h | vibhakttatA chAtvarayaiva 
siddhirvipakShasamprAptivirodhahetavaH |' iti | OM puruShArtho.ataH shabdAditi bAdarAyaNaH OM || ityatra, j~nAnasya niravadhAraNatayA mukttiM prati sAdhanatvoktteH, j~nAnasya mukttimAtrasAdhanatve cha, sambhavAt.h, brahmaj~nAnaM kiM mokShamAtrasAdhanaM uta phalAntarasyApIti sandehe, j~nAnaM mokShamAtrasAdhanamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, mokShasvargAdisamastapuuruShArthasAdhanamiti siddhAntaH | tatra, "audAyarm.h' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM sAkShAtparamparAsAdhyapradarshanapUvarkaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha j~nAnina AdAryAnmokShAdanyaphalechChAyA evAsambhavAttadukttiH prashaMsAmAtramiti vAchyam.h  |
|| nacha j~nAnina iti || audAryAt.h virakttatvAt.h, buddhayA vivekena, mokShAdanyaphaletyetatsaptamyantaM sat.h audAryAdityanenApi sambaddhayate | tadukttiH "j~nAnAdeva svargaH' ityAdirUpA j~nAnasya mokShetarapuruShArthasAdhanatvokttiH, prashaMsAmAtram.h j~nAnasya prashastatvaj~nApanaparairevetyarthaH | tathAcha, "parIkShya lokAn.h' ityAdishrutismR^itibhyAM j~nAninAM mokShetarapuruShArtheShu virakttatvena tadichChAbhAvasya pramitatvAt.h | "j~nAnAdeva svargaH' ityAdivAkyasya prashaMsAmAtratvasya kalpanIyatvena j~nAnasya svargAdihetutve pramANAbhAvAt.h j~nAnasya mokShamAtrasAdhanatvAnnaitatsarvathApAdyamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "shabdAH' ityanena shrutau, vishuddhasatvo j~nAnI yaM yaM lokaM manasA yadIchChati, tiMrha taMtaM lokaM prApnotIti vyavasthoktayA j~nAnino virakttatvarUpaudAryavattvena mokShAtirikttaphalechChAbhAvAditi sUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "vyavasthitiH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- 
prAyasho na sambhavatyeva | kasya chitsaubharyAdivadbhavati chejj~nAnenaivAsheShamIpsitaM bhavatIti vyavasthopapatteH || 1 || 2 ||
|| prAyasha iti || na sambhavatyeva j~nAnino mokShAnyaphalechCheti vartate | kasyachijj~nAninaH saubharyAdInAmanekadehadhAraNena strIbhogAdimokShetarapuruShArthechChAyAH purANeShu bhavatItyanena prakAreNa "parIkShya lokAn.h karmachitAn.h brAhmaNo nirvedamAyAt.h | prajahAti yadA kAmAn.h sarvAnpArtha manogatAn.h' ityAderj~nAninAM vairAgyapratipAdakashrutismR^ityAdivAkyasya prAyeNa j~nAninAM svargechChAbhAvaparatvena, "yaM yaM lokaM manasA saMvibhAti vishuddhasatvaH' ityAdij~nAninAmapi mokShAdanyaphalechChApratipAdakasya shrutyAdivAkyasya cha j~nAnasyAsheShapuruShArthasAdhanatvasiddheH sarvathA tadApAdyamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "shabdAH' ityanenaiva vyavasthApratipAdakashrutigrAhakeNa sUchitaH |) || 1 || OM asArvatrikI OM || ityatra, laukikasAdhane sarvAdhikArikatvaikAdhikArikatvapratItyA brahmaj~nAnaM sarvAdhikArikaM na veti sandehe, sarvAdhikArikamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, neti siddhAntaH | yadyapyetadadhikaraNasambandhitvena tatashcha j~nAnaphalasya mokShasya nirduHkhAnandadyAtmakatvarUpaudAryAtsarveShAM tadarthitvasambhavAtsarveShAmapi shravaNAdisAmarthyAttadupayogividhatvarUpaudAryAdarthI samartho vidvAn.h "uchchAvachashakttiH' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradasharnapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati-

|| nachAdhikAra iti || nanu "prAj~nAntarapR^ithaktavavaddR^iShyiH' iti j~nAnatAratamyasyokttatvAttadadhikAre.api tAratamyaM kalpanIyamityata ukttam.h- adhikAre same.apIti || tathAchAdhikAre svAbhAvike same.api teShAmadhikAriNAmuchchAvachashakttirUpAdyayogAt.h upAyAdeva phalabhedasya j~nAnalakShaNaphalatAratamyasyopapatteH | phalabhedasya kalpakatvAbhAvAdadhikArivisheShasya bhaktayAdimatvalakShaNasyAdhikArasya yo visheShastasya svAbhAvikadevatvarShitvamanuShyottamatvarUpasya kalpanaM vyarthamityarthaH | 
evaMchAdhikAriNAmuchchAvachashakttiyogAjj~nAnatAratamyasyopapatterekaprakAra eva j~nAnAdhikAra iti na j~nAnamatishayavaditi neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH phalabhedenAdhikArabhedaM samarthayatodAhR^itasUtreNa phalabhedasyochchAvachashaktayaivopapatteradhikArabhedakalpanasUchakena sUchitaH | ) taddhetutvena "avisheShaH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- bhaktayAdIti || AdipadenAdhyayanAdikaM gR^ihyate | shAstrAt.h vichAritAt.h dhyAnadvArA phalasya j~nAnasya prAptiH | sarveShAM devAnAmadhikAriNAmavisheShAdavishiShyatvAnnatvekasyApi bhaktayAdyadhikArAnusAreNa phalaprAptiH | yena vyabhichArAdbhaktayAdyadhikArasya j~nAnakAraNatA na syAdityarthaH | yadvA sarveShAM devAdInAM j~nAnasyeti sheShaH | avisheShaprasaN^gAdbhaktayAdyadhikArAnusAreNaiva shAstrAtphalaprAptergrAhyatvAdityarthaH | bhaktayAdyadhikAratAratamye kAryavaichityarUpamanumAnamuktavA pratyakShamapyAha-

|| dR^ishyamAnatvAchcheti || yadvA "atha' ityAdishrutAviti sheShaH | anumAnapUrvapakShokttAnyathAsiddhiM pariharati- uchchAvachashaktteriti || tannibandhanatvAt.h bhaktayAdyadhikAratAratamyanibandhanatvAt.h, adhikAratAratamyamantareNa tatkAraNAbhAvAditi bhAvaH | yathokttaM prAk.h | "svAdhikArAdhiko yatnaH prAyasho nopapadyate | kathaJNchidadhike yatne doShaH kashchitsamApated.h' iti | evaMcha visheShaprasaN^gAdadhikAratAratamyAnusAreNa j~nAnaprAptiriti sampUrNaj~nAnAdhikArasya sarvasulabhatvAbhAvAtsAtishayaM taditi bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyo "visheShAt.h' ityasyAvR^ittau satyAmadhikArasya visheShaj~nAnasya visheShaH syAdityarthakenokttam.h |) || 3 || OM stutaye.anumitirvA OM || ityatra, loke sadasatpravR^ittyA "visheShadarshanAttulyaM tu' ityuktayA cha bhagavajj~nAniShu sadasatpravR^ittyA visheSho.asti vA na veti sandehe, neti pUrvaH pakShaH, astIti siddhAntaH | tatra, "AtmasvarUpadArDhyam.h' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati-

|| nacha j~nAninAmiti || AtmasvarUpadArDhyAt.h AtmasvarUpAvirbhUtAnandAdilakSharasya dArDhyAt.h nishchitatvAt.h, satpravR^ittiviparItapravR^ittyoravisheShaH ityatra, loke.arthAdisAdhanasyAdhikAryanadhikAriprApyatvadarshanAdbhagavadaparokShaj~nAnaM kimadhikAribhireva prApyate, utAnadhikAribhirapIti sandehe.anadhikAribhirapi prApyata iti pUrvaH pakShaH, phale.api aparokShaj~nAne, brahmAdidevatApade chetyarthaH | sAdhanasamuchchaye.apishabdaH | chaitanyAvisheSha samuchchaye vA | adhikAramAtraprApyatvalakShaNavisheShAbhAvaH | ayaM bhAvaH | j~nAnaM devatApadaM chAdhikAribhireva prApyamiti na niyamaH | vedAdyanadhikAriNAmapi prayatnena vedAdiprApterdarshanAt.h | "svadharmaniShThaH shatajanmabhiH pumAnviriJNchatAmeti' ityAdinA devatApadAdeH prayatnasAdhyatvoktteshchamahAprayatnena sarvaiH prApuM shakyatvAt.h | nanu devatvAdikaM svAbhAvikamiti chenna, prayatnasAdhyatvashravaNena chaitanyavyatirikttasya svAbhAvikatvAbhAvAt.h | chaitanyasya sarvasAmyAt.h | svAbhAvikatve.apyautpattikakShatriyatvAbhibhavena vishvAmitrasya mahAprayatnasAdhyavipratvavanmahatA prayatnena svabhavAbhibhavena j~nAnapadayorayogyairapi prApyatvAtteShAmapi mokShaprasaN^ga iti neti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH "sarvathApi' ityanenAtmasvarUpasyAtmAvyabhichAritasyechChAprayatnAderdArDhyasya mahattvasyAprayojakatvaM vadatA sUchitaH |) yadvA, "sarvathA' apIti (sarvAthartvAditi) sUtre jIvasvabhAvasya nAnAprakAratvoktayA sUchitaH |) (ayaM cha nyAyo "nachAdhikArikam.h' ityanena devatApadaM nAkAN^kShyamiti vadatA sarvajIvAnAM nijasvabhAvashchaitanyamekaprakArameveti devAdipadaM yogyaprApyamiti sUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "niShedhasAmAnyavidhikriyANAM vibhakttatA' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- 
niShedhasAmAnyavidhikriyANAM vibhakttatvAt.h | nAdevo devapadamanvichChedanvichChanyAtyadharaM tamaH | 
|| niShedheti || ayaM bhAvaH | j~nApadayoradhikArimAtraprApyatvamiti niyama eva, tatprayojakachaitanyavyatirikttadevatvAderapi svAbhAvikatvAt.h | nacha prayatnena svAbhAvikasyAbhibhavaH, "daivImeva' ityAdishrutyAdinAnabhibhavasya pramitatvAt.h | devadInAM niShedhasAmAnyavidhikriyAvibhAgena prayatnasyaivAyogAt.h | kasyachit.h kathaM chitprayatnechChAdau virochanAdibhirmithyAj~nAnasyaiva prApteH "na devapadamanvichChed.h' ityAdinA pAtAdyanarthoktteshcheti | devatApadaviShaye vidhiniShedhasAmAnyakriyAvibhAgaparAH shrutIrudAharati-

uttarAdhikaraNe, "ato j~nAnamapyayogyaprApyam.h' iti |) || 5 || (ayaM cha nyAyo "na chAdhikArikam.h' iti, "upapUvarmapi' iti, "bahistu' iti sUtratrayasya phalapradaM, prajAnAM veti sandehe, devAnAmeveti pUrvaH pakShaH, devAdInAM prajAnAmapIti siddhAntaH | tatra, "svAtantyam.h' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatphalapradarshanapUrvakaM nacha svAtantAddevAnAmeva j~nAnAdiphalaM, na kiJNchidanyeShAmiti vAchyam.h "tvarayaiva manuShyANAM siddhiratvarayaiva tu |

cha svAmina eva phaladarshanAditi bhAvaH | evakAravyAvartyamAha- na kiJNchiditi || anyeShAM prajArUpakartR^iNAM karturapyasvAminaH phalAbhAvadasharnAditi bhAvaH nAnyeShAmiti vakttavye yannakiJNchidanyeShAmityAha, tena chetanAdirUpeNApi na prajAnAM j~nAnaphalaM, pR^ithagdIyamAnatvAditi sUchayati | evaMcha devAnAmeva svAtantAtteShAmeva phalaprAptirityaniyamaH sarveShAmityukttAnupapattiriti neti bhAvaH | taddhetutvena "atvarayaivasiddhiH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM pramANodAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- tvarayaiveti || devAnAmatvarayA siddhau nimittamAha- 
devAnAM tatprasAdena mukttireva  satAM nR^iNAmiti mAnuShamukttayarthameva devAnAmatvarayA siddhishruteH || 7 ||  
|| tatprasAdeneti || tatprasAdena teShAM devAnAM, prasAdena  indriyAdipreraNena muktyarthameveti | (anena "muktayA eva' iti tAdarthye chatutharItyukttaM bhavati |) devAnAM tvarayA siddhau manuShyamuktayarthameva devAnAmatvarayA siddhermanuShyANAmapi j~nAnaphalamokShaprAptirityukttaM bhavati |) || 7 || OM kR^itsnabhAvAttu gR^ihiNopasaMhAraH OM || ityatra, loke samaviShamaphalopetapuruShadarshanAdAnamabhedabhinnA manuShyAH kiM sarve.api mokShe samA, uta tAratamyopetA iti sandehe gR^ihastho mukttAvuttama iti pUrvaH pakShaH, sarvAshramiShu yatirevottama iti siddhAntaH | tatra "apUrNavisheShayogyatA' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha gR^ihasthAnAmasheShakarmavisheShayogyatvAdAdhikyaM mukttau tvarayaiva gR^ihiNaH sAdhayanti mukttimatvarayaiva yatayastebhyashchAtvarayAdevAsteShu cha brahmA | tadeSha shlokaH | shataM parAnabhipashyaiva devaM brahmAcharaddushcharaM yattapo.agyram.h | vihAya rAgaM manasashchopariShThaM tato.abhavatparameShThI samukttAviti | yo hi tvarayA sAdhayetsa mandaM sukhamApnuyAt.h | yo hyatvarayA sa mahaditi shrutergR^ihibhyo yatInAM tebhyo devAnAmatvarayA siddheH | bahukAlasAdhanAdbahukarmAdhikAramAtrasya durbalatvAt.h || 8 || 
|| nacha gR^ihasthAnAmiti || "apUrNatA' ityasyArtho.asheSha iti | na hyanyAshramiNAM kR^itvAdAvadhikAro.astIti  bhAvaH | evaMchApUrNakarmavisheShayogyatvAdgR^ihasthAnAmevottamatvamiti na j~nAnamatishayitamiti neti bhAvaH | taddhetutvena "atvarayaiva siddhiH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM shrutyudAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- tvarayaiva gR^ihiNa iti || deveShu madhye chaturmukhasyAtvarayaiva siddhipradarshanArthaM shlokaH | shataMparAniti manasashcha rudrAdapyupariShyaH sa prasiddho brahmA devaM viShNumabhipashyaiva j~nAnaM parAn.h brahmakalpAn.h manaso rAgaM vihAya dushcharaM tapo.agyraM yadyasmAdAcharat.h, tato mukttau parameShThI sAyujyabhAttavAdyatishayavAnabhavaditi yojanA | atvaropapAdanArthamaparokShaj~nAnaprAkttanatapovyAvR^ittyarthamabhipashyaivetyevakAraH | etAvatApi kathaM yatInAM gR^ihasthebhyaH uttamatvamityata ukttam.h- yohIti || nanu yatInAM tapaHkAlabAhulyavadgR^ihasthAnAM karmabAhulyAtsAmyameva syAdityata  Aha- bahukAleti || gR^ihiNAM bahukarmAdhikAramAtrasadbhAve.api tadAcharaNaniyamAbhAvAditi bhAvaH | anena pUrvapakShahetorbAdhitaviShayamukttaM bhavati | evaMcha yatimokShasyAtvarayaiva siddherj~nAnaprachurANAM yatInAmevottamatvamiti yuktto j~nAnasyAtishaya iti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo gR^ihasthamokShApekShayA yatimokShasyatvarayaivasiddheryatInAmevottamatvamityabhipretya tatra bAdhakamuddharatA "kR^itsnabhAvAd.h' iti sUtreNa sUchitaH |) || 8 || OM anAviShkurvannatvayAt.h OM || ityatra brahmopadeshasyAviShkAreNa gopyena chopapatterbrahmaviShayakAparokShaj~nAnasAdhanamAviShkAreNopadeShyavyaM, naveti sandehe, AviShkAreNeti pUrvaH pakShaH, neti siddhAntaH | tatra "apUrNavisheShayogyatA' ityukttameva pUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati-

na hyevaM tvaramaNo siddhirbhavati | ayogyAnAmapi shravaNaprasaN^gAt.h | tasmAdvichArya yogyAnAmevAtvarayaiva kathayitvA siddhibharvati | tyaktavA tvarAM brahmavidyAM vadeta janAya yogyAya sadaiva vidvAniti shruteH | mAnastenebhya ityAdeshcha || 9 || 
|| nahyevamiti ||  vyAkhyAnasya vyAkhyAturvisheShaj~nAnahetutvAttena chAparokShaj~nAnadvArA mukttirUpasiddhisambhavAtsambhAchatvarAdau vyAkhyArUpatvarAkareNesiddhiH kuto na bhavatItyata Aha- ayogyAnAmapIti || ayogyeShUpadeshasyAnarthahetutvena na siddhihetutvamiti bhAvaH | tarhi kena prakAreNopadeshe siddhirbhavatItyata Aha- tasmAditi vichAryAdhikArideshakAlAdhikam.h | yogyAnAmeva j~nAnasyetyarthaH | vichArashcha tvarayA na bhavatItyatvarayaivetyukttam.h | kathitvA, sthitasya puruShasya siddhirbhavatItyarthaH | atra pramANamAha- tyaktaveti || yogyAyaivetyevashabdasambandhe, ayogyAya na vadedityarthAtsiddhayati | yogyeShvevopadeshaH kartavyA 
nAyogyeShvityatra spaShyapramANamAha- mAna iti || Adishabdena "mAnastenebhyo ye abhidruhaspade nirAmiNo ripavo.anneShu jAgR^idhuH | yeShAM naitannAparaM kiM cha naikaM brahmaNaspate brUhi tebhyaH kadAchit.h | atho shamenoparatA manuShyA ye dharmiNo brUhi tebhyaH sadA naH | AdevAnAmohate vivrayo hR^idi bR^ihaspate na paraH sAmno viduH' iti R^igdvayagrahaNam.h | tasyArthaH | etadvAyuM prati vidyAdevatAnAM prArthanam.h | drohAspade.andhe tamasi sthAtuM yogyA rAmaviruddhAH | ata eva tasya ripavo jAgR^idhuH | bhogeShvAkAN^kShAvantaH | yeShashametatparaM brahma tadavaraM cha jagannAsti | kintu kiM cha naikaM nigaruNaM brahmAnirvAchyaM cha jagattebhyaH asmAn.h kadAchinmA brUhi | kiM nAma ye shamena viShNuniShThayoparatAH tasminneva ratA ye cha devAnAM vivrayaH varatve sati niyAmakaM brahmA varashchAsau yaH niyAmakashcheti vigrahaH | vakArasthAkAralopo nivarchanatvAt.h "saptasu prathamA' iti dvitIyAyAH prathamA | hR^idi vyohate samyagvahanti | sAmnastatpratipAdyAt.h brahmaNaH paraH paraM cha na viduH |  tebhyo no.asmAn.h sadA brUhIti | yadvA mAnastenebhya iti R^igdvayapratIkagrahaNam.h | Adipadena vidyAhavai brAhmaNamAjagAmetyAdergrahaNam.h | evaMcha tvarayaiva
