aihikamapraratatapratibandhe taddarshanAt.h OM || ityatra, kR^iShyAdisAdhane sAdhanAnuShThAna janmanyeva yAgAdisAdhane cha janmAntare phaladarshanAchChravaNAdisAdhanaM svasampattijanmanyevAparokShaj~nAnasAdhanaM kiM janmAntare iti sandehe, svasampattijanmanyeveti pUrvaH pakShaH, svasampattijanmani janmAntare cheti siddhAntaH | tathA, OM evaM mukttiphalAniyamastadavasthAvadhR^itestadavasthAvadhR^iteH OM || ityatra, adR^iShyaphalasya sAdhanotpattijanmani janmAntare cha darshanAjj~nAnasAdhyo mokShaH kiM yachCharIre j~nAnamutpannaM tatpAtAnantarameva bhavati, uta neti sandehe, yaddehe j~nAnamutpannaM taddehapAtAnantarameveti pUrvaH pakShaH, taddehapAtAnantaraM dehAntaraM prApya tatpAtAnantaramapIti siddhAntaH | etadadhikaraNadvayasambandhitvena "virodhahAniH' itayukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUvarkaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati-
nacha virodhAbhAvAtsAdhanAnuShThAnajanmanyeva aparokShaj~nAnaM mukttishcheti niyamaH pratibandhe sati tannirAsenAtvarayaiva siddhayupapatteH |
|| nacha virodhAbhAvAditi || pratibandharUpavirodhAbhAvAdityarthaH | sAdhanapadenAparokShaj~nAnasAdhanaM shravaNAdikaM mukttisAdhanamaparokShaj~nAnaM cha grAhyam.h | shravaNAdij~nAnasAdhanApekShayA anuShThAnetyukttam.h | sampUrtiparaM vA | mukttishchetyatra, janmanyeveti sAmIpyAdhikaraNe saptamI | niyama iti niShkAraNam.h | kAraNe sati kAryAnudaye kadApyanudayaH syAditi bhAvaH | evaMcha virodhahAnyA aihikatvena prApyasya j~nAnasya tasminneva janmanyanudayAdanudaya iva taddehapAtAnantarameva prApyasya mokShasya taddehapAtAnantaramevAbhAvAtkadApi sa na syAdityaniyama ityukttavyAghAta iti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH AdyAdhikaraNe "aprastutapratibandhaH' ityanena prArabdhakarmapratibandhakAbhAve sAdhanasampattijanmanyeva j~nAnaM bhavatIti vadatA sUchitaH | dvitIyAdhikaraNe tu, "evam.h' iti sUtrAMshenAprastutapratibandha ityarthakena pUrvavatsUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "atvarayaiva siddhiH' ityukttameva siddhAntanyAyamadhikaraNadvayasambandhitvena vivR^iNoti- pratibandhe satIti || prArabdhakarmaNA pratibandhe jAte karmaNi pratibandhake vidyamAne vetyarthaH | atrAtvarayaivetyevakAraH pratibandhasadbhAvasthalApekShayeti j~nAtavyam.h | siddhipadena j~nAnasya mokShasya cha grahaNam.h | j~nAnotpatyaniyame pramANamAha- yadyArabdhaM karma nibandhakaM syAtpretyaiva pashyedyogamevAnvavekShyetyAdishruteH | anekajanmasaMsiddhastato yAti parAM gatimiti bhagavadvachanam.h || 10 || 11 || 
|| iti shrImannyAyavivaraNe tR^itIyAdhyAyaH || 
|| yadyArabdhamiti || nibandhakaM pratibandhakaM, pretyaiva janmAntaraM prApyaiva, yogamevAnvavekShya punaH kiJNchichChravaNAdikamapyapekShya, brahma pashyedityanvayaH | muktayutpattiniyame pramANamAha- anekajanmeti || anekajanmasu saMsiddha aparokShaj~nAnI san.h sthitaH | evaM "mukttiphalAniyamaH' ityadhikaraNasya pUrvAdhikaraNAtideshAdhikaraNatvAdadhikaraNadvaye ekenaiva vAkyena pUrvottarapakShanyAyavivaraNaM kR^itamiti j~nAtavyam.h | dvitIyAdhikaraNotthAnaM tu pUrvAdhikaraNavat.h pratibandhakasatvanishchayAbhAvAbhimAnena pUrvapakShotthAnAdupapadyate | evaMcha yathA j~nAnasya pratibandhakasadbhAve.atvarayaiva siddheH pratibandhakAbhAve svasampattijanmanyevetivat.h aihikatvAnmokShasyApi pratibandhakasadbhAve.atvarayaiva siddheH pratibandhakAbhAve taddehapAtAnantarameva jAyamAnatvAdukttaM yukttamiti bhAvaH |(ayaM cha nyAyaH Adye "aprastutapratibandhaH' ityanena prArabdhakarmapratibandhe.atvarayaiva siddherbhavatIti sUchitaH | dvitIye tu, "evam.h्.h' ityanena pUrvavatsUchitaH |) || 10 || 
|| iti shrImannyAyavivaraNabhAvabodhe tR^itIyAdhyAyaH || 
phalapratipAdake.asminnadhyAye pUrvabhAvikarmakShayAkhyamokShapratipAdanArtho.ayaM pAdaH pravR^ittaH | etatpAdIyAdhikaraNapUrvapakShasiddhAntanyAyA 
anuvyAkhyAyAM saN^graheNokttAH | "sushakyatA shashvadatiprasiddhirvivekavinyAsavichArasaMj~nAH | nAnApravR^ittiH kR^itakR^ityatA cha vipakShakartAH samatItapAde | mahAphalatvaM pravivikttatA cha sandhigrahaH sAdhanamAptakR^ityam.h | visheShakAryaM kR^itasaMsthitishcha suyukttayo nirNayagAH svapakShe ||' OM AvR^ittirasakR^idupadeshAt.h OM || ityatra, ubhayavidhasAdhanadarshanena shravaNAdikaM  kiM sakR^idanuShTheyam.h, utAvartanIyamiti sandehe, jyotiShThomAdivatsakR^idanuShTheyamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, vrIhyavaghAtavadAvartanIyamiti siddhAntaH | tatra "sushakyatA' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati-
nacha shravaNAdyanAvR^ittyAparokShaj~nAnodaye sarveShAM sushakyatvamiti guNaH mahAphalatvAtsarveShAmashakyatAyA evopapannatvAt.h | anyathA sarvasushakyasyaiva sAdhanatayA sarveShAM mokShApatteH || 1 || 
|| nacha shravaNAdIti || aparokShaj~nAnodaye.abhyupagate satIti sheShaH | sushakyatvaM j~nAnasyeti sheShaH | evaMcha shravaNAdyanAvR^ittyAparokShaj~nAnAbhyupagame sakR^ichChravaNAdyanuShThAnasya sarvasaulabhyena sushakyatvaguNalAbhAttAdR^ishashravaNAdinA chAparokShaj~nAnAbhAvAnna shravaNAdikamaparokShaj~nAnasAdhanamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH "AvR^ittiH' ityanena sarveShAM sushakyatvAdanAvR^ittyaiva j~nAnamiti sUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "mahAphalatvam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- mahAphalatvAditi || j~nAnasyeti sheShaH | mahatphalaM yeneti vigraho draShyavyaH | j~nAnasya mahAphalatve.api sarvasushakyatA kuto nopapannetyata Aha- anyatheti || evaMcha mahAphalatvAjj~nAnasya shravaNAdyAvR^ittisAdhyatvamiti yukttaM shravaNAdeH j~nAnasAdhanatvamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "asakR^idupadeshAt.h' ityanena shravaNAdInAmaj~nAnanivR^ittirUpamahAphalatvAbhAve.asakR^idupadesho.api na syAditi sUchitaH |) || 1 || OM Atmeti tUpagachChanti grAhayanti cha OM || ityatra, upAsanasya nityashaH, kartavyatvena guNAntarapratItyA chAtmatvaM nityasha upAsyaM na veti sandehe neti pUrvaH pakShaH, nityasha upAsyamiti siddhAntaH | tatra "shashvadatiprasiddhiH' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha shashvadatiprasiddhatvAdAtmashabdoditaM svAmitvaM na nityasha upAsyam.h anyebhyo.adhikaphalatvena savisheShatvAdAtmatvasya || 1 || 
|| nacha shashvaditi || svAmitvamiti || harerjagatIti sheShaH | shashvadatiprasiddhasya nityamupAsanaM vyarthameva, kiM tvaprasiddaguNopAsanasya jyAyastvena tadeva nityashaH kartavyamiti bhAvaH | phalasambandhaH sphuTaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH, "AtmashabdaprayogAdevAtmashabdo.aditasvAmitvasya shashvadatiprasiddhatvAditi sUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "prativikttatA' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM sahetukaM vivR^iNoti- ayogya iti || anyebhyaH upAsitAnandAdiguNebhyaH, adhikaphalatvena svAvaratvasvAmitvalakShaNAdhikaphalatvena, AnandAdivatsvAmitvasya sakalamukttasAdhAraNyAditi bhAvaH | anena prasiddhasyApi phalAnusAreNopAsyatvAchChashvadaprasiddhernaprayojakatvamukttaM bhavati | tathA cha pravivakttatA nAma savisheShatvamiti vivaraNaM kR^itamiti j~nAtavyam.h | evaMcha prativivikttatvAdAtmatvasya sarvadopAsyatvamiti | (ayaMcha nyAyo.avadhAraNArthaka tushabdena guNAntaraparityAgenAtmatvasyaivApAsyatvoktayA, sUchitaH |) OM na pratokena hi saH OM || ityatra, "nAma brahma' iti shrutyA pramANasiddhabhedena cha nAma vAgAdikaM bhagavatpratIkaM kiM brahmatvenopAsyaM, na veti sandehe, upAsyamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, neti siddhAntaH | tatra "vivekaH' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatphalapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
tarhi visheShatvAdeva pratIkamapIshvara ityupAsyamiti na | 
|| tarhIti || nanu guNopAsanasyAvashyakatvasamarthanaparAdhikaraNayormadhye kathamasyAdhikaraNasya pravesha ityataH pUrvAdhikaraNasiddhAntarItyaitadadhikaraNapUrvapakShotthAnena saN^gatisambhavAnmadhye nivesha iti j~nApayituM tarhItyAdyukttam.h- visheShavatvAditi || "nAmabrahmetyupAste yAvannAmnopagataM tatrAsya kAmachAro bhavati' iti shruteH pratIke brahmatvopAsanasya phalAdhikyasambhavena visheShavatvAdityarthaH | yathA pUrvAdhikaraNe prasiddhayAderaprayojakatvamuktavA phalamAtrasyopAsanAprayojakatvenopAsanaM samarthitam.h | tathAtrApi pratIke brahmatvopAsanasya phalasambhavAtphalasyaivopAsanAprayojakatvena bhedAderaprayojakatvAtpratIkaM brahmatvenopAsyamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "na pratIkaH' ityanena pratIke brahmadR^iShyiM niShedhatA "yAvannAmnopagatam.h' ityAdivisheShaphalatvAtpratIke brahmadR^iShyiH kAryeti sUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "sandhigrahaH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti-
tatra sandhirupapattirvidyate tasyaiva grAhyatvAt.h anyasyeshatvagrahaNasya mithyAj~nAnatvAdevAnupapatteH || 3 || 
|| tatreti || anena sandhinopapatyA grahaH aN^gIkAra iti vivR^ito bhavati | tathApi prakR^ite kimAyAtamityata Aha- anyasyeti 
|| pratIke brahmatvopAsanasya grAhyatve, upapattirnAstIti bhAvaH | nanu phalAdhikyarUpopapatterukttatvAtkathaM netyato.apyAha- anyasyeti || IshvarAdanyasyetyarthaH | anupapatteH phalasyeti bhAvaH | upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | anarthaphalAchcheti draShyavyam.h | evaMchopapannasyaiva grAhyatvAtpratIke brahmatvopAsanasyAnupapannatvAtsakalasvAmitvena bhagavadupAsanaM yukttamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "nahi saH' ityanena pratIke brahmatvadR^iShyeryukttiviruddhatvAditi vadatA yukttiyukttasyaiva grAhyatvAditi sUchanena sUchitaH |) || 3 || OM brahmadR^iShyirutkarShAt.h OM || ityatra, upAsyAnupAsyaguNadarshanena bhUmatvarUpaM brahmatvaM sarvadopAsyaM na veti sandehe, neti pUrvaH pakShaH, sarvadopAsyamiti siddhAntaH | tatra, "vinyAsaH' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha pratidinaM vividhaguNanyAsena bhagavatprItyupapatterna bahmatAdR^iShyiniyama iti vAchyam.h | 
|| na cha pratidinamiti || vItyasyArtho vividheti | nyAseneti upasaMhR^ityopAsanenetyarthaH | bhagavatprItyupapatteriti sArvakAlikabrahmatopAsanasyApi bhagavatprItireva phalamiti bhAvaH || brahmateti || anena sUtre brahmapadaM bhAvapradhAnamityukttaM bhavati | AtmatvopAsananiyamavat.h brahmatvopAsanAyAmapi niyamaH kiM na syAdityata ukttam.h- niyama iti || tadvadatra visheShahetvabhAvAditi bhAvaH | evaMcha bhUmatvasya sadopAsyatvAbhAvAdukttajyAyastvamayukttamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH "brahmadR^iShyiH' ityanena brahmatvopAsanasyAvashyakartavyatvaM samarthayatA sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "sAdhanam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- 
asheShaguNAntarbhAvena tasyaivAdhikasAdhanatvAt.h || 4 ||
|| asheSheti || brahmatva iti sheShaH | atra sarvaguNAnAM hi yato.antarbhAva iShyata iti vachanAttasyaiva brahmatvopAsanasyaivAdhikasAdhanatvAt.h guNAntaropAsanApekShayAdhikaprasAdahetutvAdityarthaH | evaMcha brahmatvopAsanasyaivAdhikasAdhanatvAt.h  brahmatvaM sadopAsyamiti yukttamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH, "utkarShAt.h' ityanena sarvaguNAntarbhAvena brahmatvasyaivokttatvAditi vadatA sUchitaH |) || 4 || OM AdityAdimatayashchAN^ga upapatteH OM || ityatra, sadopAsyAnupAsyaguNadarshanAtsvotpAdakAN^gAshritatvena devairupAsanaM sarvadA kartavyaM na veti sandehe, neti pUrvaH pakShaH, sadA kartavyamiti siddhAntaH | tatra, "vichAraH' ityukttapUvarpakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha vividhasthAneShvAdityAdInAM charaNAdviShNvaN^geShvAdityAdimatiniyamo nAstIti vAchyam.h | tatkR^itAveva kR^ityasyAptatvAdAdityAdInAm.h || 5 ||
|| nacha vividhasthAneShviti || vItyasyArtho vividhasthAneShviti | sUryAdidevAnAM vividhasthAneShu charaNena sadA chakShurAdyaN^gAshritatvAbhAvAttathopAsanasyAnarthaphalahetutvAdityarthaH | evaMcha vichArAtsvotpAdakAN^gAshritatvena devatopAsanasyAkartavyatvAttadvadAtmatvamapi na sarvadopAsyamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH "upapatteH' ityanena vividhasthAneShu charaNe.api rUpAntareNa bhagavadaN^gAshritatvAdAdityAdyAshrayatvenopAsanamupapadyata iti vadatA sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "AptakR^ityam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- tatkR^itAviti || AdityAdidevAnAM svotpattyaN^gAshritatvenopAsanakR^itAveva tatra dehalayadvArA mokShalakShaNakR^ityasyAptatvAdApyatvAdityarthaH | devAnAM tathopAsanasyAkaraNe viShNvaN^ge layAsambhavena mokShAnupapatterityarthaH | nachAnyathopAsanaprasaN^gAdetadayukttamiti vAchyam.h | AdityAdInAM tatkR^itau vividhasthAnacharaNalakShaNakR^ityakR^itAvapi rUpAntareNa viShNvaN^garUpakR^ityasya prAptatvAditi bhAvaH | evaMchAprakR^ityatvAdbhagavadaN^gAshritadevopAsanamAvashyakamiti bhAvaH |) ayaM cha nyAyaH "upapatteH' ityanenaiva vividhasthAneShu charaNe.api rUpAntareNa bhagavadaN^gAshritatvarUpakR^ityasyAptatvAdupapadyate tathopAsanamiti vadatA sUchitaH |) || 5 || OM AsInasambhavAt.h OM ityatra, dvividhasAdhanadarshanenAsanaM sarvathApekShitaM na veti sandehe, neti pUrvaH pakShaH, sarvathApekShitamiti siddhAntaH | tatra "saMj~nA' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradasharnapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha j~nAnasya samyagviShayatvamAtreNa pUrterAsanAdinA na kAyarmiti vAchyam.h AsanAdinA nishchalatvAdivisheShakAryopapatteH || 6 || 
|| nacha j~nAnasyeti || j~nAnasyetyasya pUrterityanena sambandhaH | samyagityataH pUvarM manasa iti sheShaH | yadvA, j~nAyate.aneneti j~nAnasyetyasya manasa ityartho draShyavyaH | saM shabdArthaH samyagiti | tadviShayatveneti bhagavadviShayatvenetyarthaH | Adipadena "samaM kAyashirogrIvam.h' ityasya grahaNam.h | evaMchAsanAdyabhAve.api manaso bhagavadviShayatvamAtreNAparokShaj~nAnasambhavAdvayarthaM AsanAdIti tadupadeshAprAmANyamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "sambhavAt.h' ityanenAsane satyeva 
chittavikShepAbhAvenopAsanasambhavAttadabhAve chittavikShepAbhAvAsambhavAditi vadatA sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "visheShakAryamityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- AsanAdineti || nishchalatvAditi | manasa iti sheShaH | Adipadena, "achalatvaM chApekShya' sati sUtrAnusAreNa sharIrAchalatvaM cha grAhyam.h | manaso nishchalatvAdikaM vinA samyagbhagavadviShayatvAsambhavena j~nAnasyaivAsambhavAditi bhAvaH | evaMchAsanAdinA visheShakAryopapatterAsanAdikamAvashyakamiti na tadupadeshAprAmANyamiti bhAvaH |) || 6 || ayaM cha nyAyaH "achalatvaM chApekShya' iti sUtreNa sharIrAchalatvadvArA manaso.achalatvarUpakAryavisheShaM prati hetutvamiti vadatA sUchitaH |) || 6 || OM AprAyaNAttatrApi hi dR^iShyam.h OM || ityatra, j~nAnasAdhanatvAjj~nAninAmapi darshanAt.h  dhyAnaM kiM j~nAnaparyantamevAvashyakamuta mukttiparyantamiti sandehe, j~nAnaparyantamevAvashyakamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, mukttiparyantamapIti siddhAntaH | tatra, "nAnApravR^ittirityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nachAnyasyApi sAdhanasya kartuM shakyatvAnna yAvanmukttisAdhanaM kAryamiti vAchyam.h dhyAnaM vinAparokShaj~nAnAkhyavisheShakAyarAnupapatteH || 7 || 
|| nachAnyasyApIti || nAnetyasya vivaraNamanyasyApIti | evaMcha dhyAnAdanyasya shravaNAdisAdhanasyApyAnandAtishayArthaM kartuM shakyatvAnna tadarthaM dhyAnamAvashyakamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH "AprAyaNAt.h' ityanena j~nAnaparyantaM dhyAnaM dhyAnaviShayaM samarthayatA dhyAnaM vinA shravaNAdisAdhanAntarasyApi vakttuM shakyatvAdaniyama iti sUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "visheShakAryam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- dhyAnaM vineti || upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | dhyAnaM vinAnandAdyatishayAkhyavisheShakAyarAnupapatterityapi draShyavyam.h | tena j~nAnaparyantamavashyaM katarvyatve.api mukttiparyantatvaM kuta iti shaN^kA nirastA | AnandAtishaye dhyAnasyAntaraN^gasAdhanatvAditi bhAvaH | evaMchAnandAtishayAkhyavisheShAnmukttiparyantaM dhyAnamAvashyakamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "tatrApi hi dR^iShyam.h' ityanena phalAbhAve.api yadA dhyAnaM kartavyatvena pramitaM tadA kimu vakttavyaM phale satyavashyaM kartavyamiti | aparokShaj~nAnAtsvasvaj~nAnottarashravaNAdimAtrasAdhyayAnandAtishayasya visheShakAryasya sadbhAvAd.h dhyAnamAvashyakamiti sUchanena sUchitaH |) || 7 || OM tadadhigama uttarapUrvAghayorashleShavinAshau tadvayapadeshAt.h OM || ityatra, sakAmaniShkAmakamarNormokShasAdhanatvAsAdhanatvAdarshanAjj~nAnaM mukttisAdhanaM naveti sandehe, neti pUrvaH pakShaH, mukttisAdhanamiti siddhAntaH |  tatra "kR^itakR^ityatA' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradasharnapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha j~nAnodaye.asheShakarmakShaye kR^itakR^ityatvAttadaiva mukttiH na chetkarmakShaya iti vAchyam.h prArabdhasyaiva kR^itasya yAvAdbhogaM saMsthiteH | 
||nacha j~nAnodaya iti || tadaiva j~nAnAnantarameva, mukttiH syAditi sheShaH | na cheShyApattiH | jIvanmukttAnAmupalambhAditi bhAvaH | ApAdakasyAprayojakatvaM pariharati- nacheti || mukttirityatrApi sambaddhayate | yadi j~nAnodaye.api mukttirna syAttarhi karmakShayo na syAt.h | niShkAraNamavasthAnAyogAditi bhAvaH | nanUtpannaM j~nAnaM tadaiva na karma kShiNotItyApAdakAsiddhiM vAshaN^kaya pariharati- nachediti || j~nAnodaye.asheShakarmakShaya ityanuvartate | karmakShaya iti saptamyAH prathamAntatvena vipariNAmaH | tarhIti sheShaH | karmakShayaH kadApIti sheShaH | j~nAnasya viramyavyApArAyogAditi bhAvaH | evaMcha j~nAnenaivAsheShakarmakShaye tadaiva mukttiH syAt.h | nachaivaM tasmAtkarmaNAM pratibandhakatvena j~nAnasya mokShasAdhanatvAniyama ityukttavyAghAta iti neti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH "tadadhigamaH' iti sUtreNa j~nAnodayAnantarameva pUrvottarapuNyapApabhAvyashleShoktayA sarvakarmasambandhAbhAve kR^itakR^ityatvAttadaiva mukttiH syAditi sUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "kR^itasaMsthitiH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti-
karmANi kShapayedviShNuraprArabdhAni vidyayA | prArabdhAni tu bhogena kShapayan.h svaM padaM nayediti vachanAchcha || 8 || 
|| iti  nyAyavivaraNe chaturthAdhyAyasya prathamaH pAdaH || 
|| prArabdhasyaiveti || kR^itasya karmaNaH, yadi j~nAnodaya eva na mukttiH, tiMrha j~nAnena karmakShaya eva na prApnotItyukttamevetyAshaN^kAparihArArthamukttam.h- prArabdhasyaiveti || aprArabdhasyaiva j~nAnena nAsho na sarvasyeti bhAvaH | evaM tarhi prArabdhakarmaNa eva pratibandhakatvAnna mukttiH syAdityata ukttam.h- yAvadbhogamiti || nanu prArabdhakarmaNo bhoge na kShayo.anyasya j~nAnenetyetatkuta ityata Aha- karmANIti || evaMcha j~nAnodaye.api prArabdhasya kR^itasya yAvadbhogaM sthitatvAttadaiva mokSho na bhavatItyukttaM yukttamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "anArabdhakArye eva tu tadavadheH' bhogena tviterakShapayitvAtha sampatsyata iti sUtradvayena sUchitaH |) || 8 || 
|| iti nyAyavivaraNe bhAvabodhe chaturthAdhyAyasya prathamaH pAdaH || 
devadehalyamanuShyotkrAntipratipAdanArtho.ayaM pAdaH pravR^ittaH | etatpAdIyAdhikaraNapUrvapakShasiddhAntanyAyA anuvyAkhyAyAM saN^graheNokttAH | "vyAmishratA kAryakaratvamarthaH klR^iptiH sudArDhyaM paratantratA cha | samAnadharmaH kR^itasheShatA cha lokopamA pUvarmatAnusArAH | visheShasAmyashrutirADhyatA cha samAnalopo mahimAvisheShaH | kR^itArthatA shashvadanupravR^ittiH siddhAntanirNItivisheShahetavaH ||' OM vAN^manasi darshanAchChabdAchcha OM || ityatra, "tatpUrakatvAdvAchaH' iti vAcho manojAtatvokttivisheShapramANAdasharnAbhyAM vAN^manasi lIyate, na veti sandehe, neti pUrvaH pakShaH, manasi lIyata iti siddhAntaH | tatra, "vyAmishratA' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha vAkpUrvarUpaM mana uttararUpaM manaH pUrvarUpaM vAguttararUpaM ityukttervyAmishratvAdanirNItireva vAkpUrvarUpaM mana uttararUpaM iti vAchaH pUrvavarNadevatA tvanirdeshamAtreNa manaH pUrvaM ityanena sAmyam.h | 
|| nacha vAgiti || anirNItirvAN^manasayorniyamyaniyAmakabhAvasyeti sheShaH | tadadhInasya tatra layo vakttavyaH | evaMcha vAN^manasayorniyamyaniyAmakabhAve pratipAdakokttervyAmishratvena tadanirNayAnna manasi vAcho laya iti mokShAbhAvAdaniyama ityukttavyAghAta iti neti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH "darshanAchChabdAchcha' ityanena, "vAkpUrvarUpam.h' iti shrutyapekShayA, "manaH pUrvarUpam.h' iti shruteH sayukttikashrutyAnukUlyena patyakShAnusAritvena cha prAbalyadyotakena sUchitaH | ) taddhetutvena "visheShasAmyashrutiH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- vAkpUrvarUpamiti || iti vAchaH asya vAkyasyetyarthaH | sAmyamityanena sambandhaH | vAcho vAN^.hnAmakasya viShNoriti cha | pUrvavarNadevatAtveti | viShNuriti saMhitAyAM, ShakArAdipUrvavarNapratipAdyatvanirdeshamAtreNetyarthaH | sAmyamiti manonAmakasyApi viShNoH pUrvavarNadevatAtvopapatterityarthaH | idamukttaM bhavati | astyeva vAcho manasi layaH | nachoktayorvyAmishratvena manaHprAdhAnyAnishchayaH | atra khalu vAkpUrvarUpam.h, mana uttararUpam.h, ityAdinA viShNuriti saMhitAyAM pUrvottaravarNadevatAtve munimatavivAda uchyate  | tatra chAratUkttayoH sAmyam.h, anyatarapakShe visheShAdarshanAt.h | nacha vyAmishratApi vakttR^itvamantR^itvanimittakavAN^manaH shabdavAchyayorubhayorapi viShNurUpayoH pUvarottaravarNadevatAtvopapatteriti | nanu yadA pUrvottaravarNadevatAtve munimatavivAdastadA mAstu vyAmishratvaM vAN^manasanAmakayordevatayorguNapradhAnabhAve yadA munimatavivAdastadAstyevorvyAmishratvaM na cha tatra munimatavivAda eva nAstIti vAchyam.h | tathA satyetadvAkyadvayasya devatAviShayakatvAbhAvaprAptyA "tatpUrvakatvAdvAchaH' ityadhikaraNe bhAShye, "tasmAnmana eva pUrvarUpaM vAguttararUpamiti manaHpUrvakatvAdvAcho nAnutpattiH' ityuktayayogAdityato visheShashrutirityaMshaM vivR^iNoti- 
manasA vA agre saN^kalpayatyatha vAchA vyAharatIti yukttito visheSho manaHpUrvakatvasyaiva shruta iti prAdhAnyaM manasa eveti hi j~nAyate | sR^iShyau cha vilaye chaiva sadA pUrvapravartane | niyantR^itve cha vachase mano.adhIshaM shivo hi taditi shruteshcha || 1 || nacha manaHpUrvakatvaniyamAdasheShadR^iShyAdR^iShyavyAparANAM tasya prANAdanUnatA 
|| manaseti || yukttita iti tR^itIyAntAttasiH | manaHpUrvakatvasya "manaH pUrvarUpam.h' "vAguttararUpam.h' iti ukttasya vAcho manojanyatvasyetyarthaH | evakAreNa manaso vAkpUrvakatvasyetyasya vyavachChedaH | hishabdo hetau | tathAcha guNapradhAnabhAve munimatavivAde.api, nokttayorvyAmishratvam.h | manaHpUrvakatvasyaiva yaktayA visheShashravaNena manasa eva prAdhAnyaparij~nAnAt.h | nacha vAcho mano.adhInatve.api, devatAyAHkutastaditi vAchyam.h | achetanasyAnyonyavashatvasya devatAnimittakatvAt.h | nachAsminpakShe vAkpUrvarUpaM mana uttararUpamiti munimatasyAprAmANyApattiH, tasya pUrvottaravarNadevatAtvamAtraparatvena devatAparatvAbhAvAditi bhAvaH | manasa eva prAdhAnye pramANamAha- sR^iShyAviti | pUrvapravartane svAvarApekShayA prathamapravartana ityarthaH | vachasaH sR^iShyayAdau viShaye mano.adhInatA | manobhimAnIndrAdInAM kathaM vAgabhimAnyumAdhIshatvamityata Aha- shivo hIti || evaMcha vAN^manasayorniyamyaniyAmakabhAvasyokttarItyA nishchayasambhavAdvAcho manasi layopapatteryukttamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "shabdAchcha' ityanena, "manasA vA agre saN^kalpayati' ityuktayA vAcho manovashatvarUpavisheShapratipAdakashrutigrAhakeNokttaH | manovashatvarUpavisheShapratipAdakashrutigrAhakeNokttaH | etachchopalakShaNam.h | ubhayorapi varNadevatAtvarUpasAmyasyApi shrutatvAdityapi draShyavyam.h |) || 1 || OM tanmanaH prANa uttarAt.h OM || ityatra, prANAnmana iti manasaH prANotpannatvavisheShadasharnAbhyAM manaH prANe lIyate, na veti sandehe, neti pUrvaH pakShaH, prANe lIyata iti siddhAntaH | tatra,"kAryakaratvam.h' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- nacha mana iti || tadUnasya hi tatra layo vakttavyaH | nacha manasaH prANAdUnatvaM sambhavati | yathA prANaH sarvapravR^ittihetuH tathA mano.apyanvayavyatirekAbhyAM sarvapravR^ittikAraNaM dR^ishyate | evaMcha manasaH sarvakAryakAraNatvena prANAnUnatayA prANe layAbhAve nokttamayukttamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo.anvayavyatirekAbhyAM 
sarvapravR^ittikAraNatvena "taddarshanAt.h' iti pUrvasUtre pratipAditaM manaH, tatparAmarshakena tadityanena sUchitaH | anyathA "manaH' ityevAvakShyat.h | (taddhetutvena, "ADhyatA' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM pramANodAhaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- 
indriyasthaiH svarUpaistu j~nAnAni janayatyasau | manaHsthena visheSheNa kAmaiH karmavadeva cha | pR^ithak.hsthitena rUpeNa jIvaM dhArayati prabhuH | jIvasthitena rUpeNa vedayatyahamityapi | prANa eko vashI nityaM bAhyAntaH karaNeshvaraH | tAnyetAnyavashAnyeva tathApi kR^ipayaiva saH | pR^ithakshaktto.api tadgaistu svarUpaistadgakAryakR^it.h | tasyesho bhagavAnviShNurevameSha yathAnyagaH | ityAdishruteH prANasyaivADhyatAvagamAt.h || 2 || 
|| indriyasthairiti || indriyaisthaiH chakShurAdiniyAmakasUryAdipuMsthitaiH manaHsthena manoniyAmakarudrasthitena, rUpeNa visheSheNa, j~nAnAni janayatIti sambandhaH | manasaH sarvaj~nAnahetutvAditi bhAvaH | kAmaiH karmendriyaniyAmakadevatAgataiH, nanu prANaH kimindriyAdidevatAH parityajya, j~nAnajananAdau shaktto, navA, Adye tatrAvasthAnavaiyarthyam.h | dvitIye kathaM tasyADhyatetyata Aha- tAnIti || api yadyapi, prANaH pR^ithak.h tadvAratAmantareNa, kAryakaraNe shakttaH, tathApi, indriyaniyamanAtteShAM phalAdhikyaM bhavediti teShu kR^ipayA, avashAnyeva paratantrANyeva, dvAratvenAdAya, tadgatarUpavisheShaistadgakAryakR^it.h teShu gatakAryam.h tadgakAryaM, taiH kriyamANamiti yAvat.h | tatkarotItyarthaH | nanvevaM prANasyaiva nirupacharitasvAtantyaM, syAdityata Aha- tasyeti || evaM prANAntaHprANakAryakR^idityarthaH | anena, "so.adhyakShaH' ityatra siddhAnte pramANamukttaM veditavyam.h | evaMcha mano.apekShayA prANasyADhyatayA manasaH prANe laya ityukttaM yukttamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "prANaH' ityanena prakarSheNAnitIti rudrAdibhyo.apyatishayena cheShyakatvoktayA sUchitaH || 2 || OM so.adhyakShe tadupagamAdibhyaH OM ityatra, "saprANamasR^ijata' iti paramAtmotpannatvavisheShAdarshanAbhyAM prANaH paramAtmani lIyate na veti sandehe, neti pUrvaH pakShaH, lIyata iti siddhAntaH | tatra pUrvAdhikaraNasambandhitvenokttau "kAryakaraNatvADhyatA' rUpanyAyAvatidishati- 
so.adhyakShe ityasyApyevamevAshaN^kA parihArashcha | 
|| so.adhyakSha itIti || evamevAshaN^keti | tadUnasya hi tatra layo vakttavyaH | nacha prANasya paramAtmanaH sakAshAdUnatvaM sambhavati | "yathA viShNurhi sarvakAryakartA, tathA prANo.api | prANAdidamAvirAsIt.h' iti shrutyA sarvakAryakartA pratIyate | ato na prANaH paramAtmani lIyata iti shaN^kArthaH | parihAra iti | "sarvaM hyevaitatparamevatiShThate, prANashcha prANAshcha prANinashcha' ityAdi shrutyA prANAdapi paramAtmana ADhyatAvagamAt.h | prANasya viShNau laya ityukttaM upapannamiti parihAra ityarthaH | ayaM cha nyAyaH "adhyakShaH' ityanena prANasya sakalacheShyakatvAtparamAtmanastato.api sakalacheShyakatvarUpAdhikyapratipAdakena sUchitaH |) nanvasyAdhikaraNasya yadi pUrvAdhikaraNavadevAshaN^kAparihArau, tarhi pR^ithagArambho vyarthaH syAdityata Aha- 
shrutibAhulyameva shaN^kAyAM parihAre cha visheShahetuH || 3 || 4 || 
|| shrutibAhulyameveti || "na prANaH kiJNchidAshritaH | anadyamAno yadannamatti' ityAdishrutibAhulyaM shaN^kAyAM, sarve prANamupagachChanti prANaH paramupagachChati prANo vAvardbashitavveshaH Isho hyasau sarvasyeshitavyashcha parasya' ityAdishrutibAhulyaM visheShaheturityarthaH | tathAchAbhyadhikashaN^kAsadbhAvAnnaitadadhikaraNavaiyarthyamiti bhAvaH | nacha shrutibAhulyamavalambya shaN^kite kathaM tenaiva parihAra iti vAchyam.h | parihArabAhulyapadasya niravakAshatvopalakShakatvAt.h | pUrvapakShodAhR^itAnAM shrutInAM sAvakAshatvAditi bhAvaH | yadvA nanu "chakShurAdivattatsahashiShyayAdibhyaH' ityatra prANasya paramAtmAdhInatvasyokttatvena tadUnatvAtkathamukttarItyAtrAdhikAshaN^kA, nacha prANAdidamAvirAsIt.h' iti shrutimavalambyeyamAshaN^kA sambhavatIti vAchyam.h | "ananyeshvaratA prANe tadanyeshvaravarjanAt.h' ityAdinA tatraiva tasyAH sAvakAshatvasyokttatvAdityata Aha- shrutibAhulyamiti || ADhyatAmAtrasyokttayuktayanupamardakatvAt.h kathaM parihAra ityata Aha- parihAre cheti || shiShyaM pUrvavat.h || 3 || OM bhUteShu tachChruteH OM || nanvatrAdhikaraNe pUrvapakShasiddhAntanyAyau kuto nokttau na vivR^itau cheti chetsatyam.h | asyAdhikaraNasya "naikasmin.h darshayatau hi' ityanenAnatibhinnArthatvAt.h | tarhi prathamAtikramaNe kAraNAbhAvAdatra nyAyAvanuktavAvR^itya chottarAdhikaraNe tadukttau tadvivR^itau cha kiM nimittamiti chet.h | satyam.h | anekabhUteShu layo.arthAtsiddhayati | bhUtalamAtranirNaye tu nottarAdhikaraNokttAnekabhUteShu laya iti naikasminnityasya prAdhAnyAt.h | na chAtrApi bhUteShviti bahuvachanabalAttatsiddhiriti sAmyamiti vAchyam.h | "bhUteShu devAvilIyante' iti bhUtalayavAkyasyaikasmin.h bhUte sarveShAmapi devAnAM mukhyalayo.api tadvAreNAnyatra layopapatterasyAdhikaraNasya vivakShitalayavisheShAnirNAyakatvAt.h | nachaivaM satyetadadhikaraNaM vyarthamiti vAchyam.h, bhUteShu devA vilIyanta iti shrutisiddhavisheShasUchakatvena sArthakatvAt.h | yadvArthaklR^iptisamAnalopAvevAtra pUrvapakShasiddhAntanyAyau 
draShyavyau | tathA hi "agnau sarve devA vilIyante' iti shrutyA bhUtAntarAdhInatvena cha R^ibhvAdidevA agnAveva vilIyante bhUtAntare cha veti sandehe, agnAveva sarveShAM laya iti pUrvaH pakShaH, na kevalamagnau, pR^ithivyAdibhUtAntare.apIti siddhAntaH | tatra, "agnau sarve devA vilIyante' iti shrutyarthasya sarvadevAnAmagnau laya ityasya klR^iptatvAditi pUrvapakShanyAyAbhiprAyaH | "bhUteShu devA vilIyante' iti shrutirupamAna(sahitalopasya)sahitasya lopasya layasya grAhyatvAditi siddhAntanyAyAbhiprAyaH | (pUrvapakShanyAyastu anekabhUteShu layaM vadatA "agnau sarve devAH' iti shrutyA agnAveva laya ityasyArthasya klR^iptatvAditi sUchanena sUchitaH | ) || 4 || OM naikasmindarshayato hi OM ityatra shrutyanyAdhInatvAbhyAM devAH kimagnAveva vilIyanta uta sarveShu bhUteShviti sandehe, agnAveva vilIyanta iti pUrvaH pakShaH, sarveShu bhUteShviti siddhAntaH | tatra, "arthaklR^iptiH' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha bhUtAnAmutpattikramavaiparItyena layokttermukttilayayovirsheShAbhAvAchchaikasminneva bhUte sarveShAM layo.arthataH klR^ipta iti vAchyam.h |
|| nacha bhUtAnAmiti || "ekasmin.h bhUtaH' ityatra bhUta ityuktayAtra sUtre pUrvasUtrAdbhUteShviti vachanavipariNAmenAnuvartata ityukttaM bhavati | savareShAM devAnAmiti sheShaH | arthataH agnau sarve devA vilIyanta ityanyathAnupapatteH | nachAtrAgnAvitishrutyanyathAnupapattyA ekasmin.h bhUte sarveShAM devAnAM laya iti pUrvapakSho na yukttaH | pUrvAdhikaraNe bhUteShu devA vilIyanta iti shrutyavaShyambhena bhUteShu layasya samarthanAdityata ukttam.h- visheShAbhAvAchchetyantam.h || ekasminnagnAveva sarvadevalayAN^gIkAre.api "bhUteShu devA vilIyante' iti shrutyupapattiriti vAkyasheShaH | idamukttaM bhavati | asti tAvadbhUtAnAmutpattikramavaiparItyena layaH | "kartA prANAdikasyAsya hantA bhUmyAdikasya cha | yaH kramAdvayutkramAchchaiva sa hariH para uchyate' iti shruteH | "anurUpaH kramaH sR^iShyau pratirUpo laye kramaH' iti smR^iteshcha | utpattishchAkAshAdikrameNaiva | "Atmana AkAshaH sambhUtaH' ityAdishruteH | tathAchAgnAveva sarvadevalayAN^gIkAre.api bhUteShvityupapadyate | agnervAyau, vArorAkAshe vilayAt.h | nacha shrutismR^itI saMhAraviShaye, na mukttiviShaye iti vAchyam.h, mukttipralayayorvisheShAbhAvAditi | evaMchAtharklR^iptyAgnAveva sarvadevAnAM laya iti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH, ekasmin.h bhUte layaM niShedhatA "naikasmin.h' ityanena "bhUteShu devA vilIyante' iti shruteragnau devA vilIyante.agnirvAyau, vAyurAkAsha iti parayA bhUteShu devAnAM laya ityarthopapatterarthAdekasmin.h, na chAgnau layaH klR^ipta iti sUchanena sUchitaH |) kuto netyata Aha- 
tattadbhUtodbhavatvAttattaddevAnAM tatsamAnAnAM cha visheShavachanAbhAve svasamAnalayasthAna eva layopapatteH | visheShashruteshcha || 5 || nacha prakR^iteH saMsArAbhAvAdineshenApyanyathAkartumashakyatvena sudR^iDhatvAtsarvasAmyameveshvareNa | nachetsaMsAritvamiti yukttam.h | 
|| tattadbhUteti || yeShAM yeShAM devAnAM yasmin.h bhUte laya uchyata iti sheShaH | tathAcha tattaddevAnAM tattadbhUta eva sAkShAllayo vakttavya iti naikasminbhUte sarveShAM laya iti bhAvaH | tattadutpannAnAM yadi tatra tatra layastarhi varuNAdyanutpannAshviprabhR^itInAM varuNAdau layo na syAditi bAdhakaparihArArthaM "samAnalopaH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- tatsamAnAnAM cheti || varuNAdyutpannAbAdidevatAsamAnAnAM varuNAdyanutpannAmashviprabhR^itInAM svasamAnAbAdidevatAlayasthAne varuNAdau laya ityarthaH | kvachidevaMvidhAnAmanyatra layadarshanAtkathamayaM niyama ityata Aha- visheShavachanAbhAva iti || anena samAnalopa ityatra samAnAmityAvR^ittiH | dvitIyasamAnAnAmityasyAnantaraM layasthAna iti sheSha ityukttam.h | na kevalamidaM yukttitaH, kiM tarhItyata Aha- visheShashruteshcheti || shrutishcha "pR^ithivyAmR^ibhavaH' ityAdikA bhAShyodAhR^itA draShyavyA | anena samAnalopo visheShashrutirUpamAnasahito laya iti prakArAntareNa vivR^itaM bhavati | evaMcha tattadutpannatvenAnukttadevAnAmapi samAnalopena tattadutpannadevAnAM tatratatra laya ityukttaM yukttamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "darshayato hi' ityanena shrutyorasandigdha ityananuguNatvoktayA tattadbhUtodbhavatvAt.h tattaddevAnAM tatratatra laya ityukttisAhityena prAbalyaM sUchayan.h tatra bAdhakaparihArArthatvena sUchitaH |) || 5 || OM samAnA chAsR^ityupakramAdamR^itatvaM chAnupoShya OM ityatra, bhagavadadhInatvanityamukttatvAbhyAM prakR^itiH paramAtmanilIyate na veti sandehe lIyata iti pUrvaH pakShaH, neti siddhAntaH | tatra "sudArDhyam.h' ityukttapUrvapakShaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- nacha prakR^iteriti || nanu prakR^itiH paramAtmani lIyata iti pUrvaH pakSho na yukttaH, saMsAriNo hi muktayarthaM layaH, prakR^iteH kAmAditaratra ityatra nityamukttatvenAsaMsAritvasyokttatvAdityato.asaMsAritvebAdhakamukttam.h- nachediti || saMsAritvaM prakR^iteH | tarhi saMsArAbhAvAdinA prakAreNeshvareNa sarvasAmyaM syAditi sheShaH | nAsaMsAritvaM prakR^iterupapannam.h | tathAtve bhagavatA sarvasAmyApAtAditi bhAvaH | nanvIshvaraprakR^ityorasaMsAritve samAne.api svAtantAdiguNAntareNa vaiShamyaM syAditi na sarvasAmyamityata ukttam.h- IshenApIti || saMsArAbhAvAdinetyatrApi sambaddhayate | tena nimittena, anyathA 
svaniyamyatvAtpUrNatvAderIshenApi kartumashakyatvena svAtantyasya sudR^iDhatvAdityarthaH | tathAcha nityaM saMsArarAhitye sarvaguNopapattyA guNAntare.api vaiShamyaM na syAditi bhAvaH | sarvasAmyamiti vAkyaM, siddhAntavirodhena na chetsarvasAmyaM tarhi saMsAritvaM siddhamiti viparyayaparyavasAnaparatvenApi yojyam.h | tathAcha prakR^iteH saMsAritvAdviShNau laya iti bhAvaH | evaM prakR^iteH saMsArAbhAve IshenApyanyathAkartumashakyatvena sudR^iDhatvAdIshena sarvasAmyaM syAditi | prakR^iterapi viShNau laya iti nAdhikAriNAM prANAvasAnatvamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "amR^itatvaM chAnupoShya' ityanena prakR^itenirtyamukttatveneshenApyanyathAkartumashakyatvena sudR^iDhatvamiti sUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "mahimA' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- IshenApIti || saMsArAbhAvAdinetyatrApi sambaddhayate | tena nimittena, anyathA svaniyamyatvAtpUrNatvAderIshenApi kartumashakyatvena svAtantyasya sudR^iDhatvAdityarthaH | tathAcha nityaM saMsArarAhitye sarvaguNopapattyA guNAntare.api vaiShamyaM na syAditi bhAvaH | sarvasAmyamiti vAkyaM, siddhAntavirodhena na chetsarvasAmyaM tarhi saMsAritvaM siddhamiti viparyayaparyavasAnaparatvenApi yojyam.h | tathAcha prakR^iteH saMsAritvAdviShNau laya iti bhAvaH | evaM prakR^iteH saMsArAbhAve IshenApyanyathAkartumashakyatvena sudR^iDhatvAdIshena sarvasAmyaM syAditi | prakR^iterapi saMsAritvena viShNau laya iti nAdhikAriNAM prANAvasAnatvamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "amR^itatvaM chAnupoShya' ityanena prakR^iternityamukttatveneshenApyanyathAkartumashakyatvena sudR^iDhatvamiti sUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "mahimA' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- 
Ishvarasya mahAmahimatvAt.h | nityamasaMsAritvasya nityaM tadanugraheNaivopapatteH | sadAnityatayAnityaM nityaM nityAtmanA yataH | nityayaiva svashaktayesho niyAmayati nityadA | dravyaM karma cha kAlashcha svabhAvashchetanAdhR^itiH | prakR^itiH puruShashchaiva na santi yadupekShayetyAdishruteshcha || 6 || 
|| Ishvarasyeti || OM tadapIteH saMsAravyapadeshAd.h' ityAdisUtrokttamochakatvasUkShmatvaj~nAnAnandAdiguNAdhikyarUpamahAmahimatvAdIshvarasya na prakR^iterIshvareNa sAmyamityarthaH | nanvasaMsAritve guNAntareNa vaiShamyaM na sambhavatItyata Aha- nityamiti || tadadhInatvenAsaMsAritve kathaM na sAmyApAdanamiti bhAvaH | yadvA mahAmahimatvenaiveshvareNa sAmyAbhAve prakR^iteH saMsAritvamapi syAdityata Aha- nityamiti || nityasaMsAritvasya kathamIshvarAdhInatvamityata ukttam.h- tadanugraheNeti || nityasyApi bhagavadadhInatve pramANamAha- sadeti || yato yathAnityaM ghaTAdikamanityatayeshvaraH sadA niyAmayati, kadAchidapi na nityaM karoti | tathAnityaM prakR^ityAdikaM nityAtmanA svashaktayaiva nityadA niyAmayati, na jAtvanityaM karotItyarthaH | nanvetadalaukikamiti chenna, nityakarmabhirduritaprAgabhAvAnuvR^itteH | sAdhyatvena vAdibhirabhyupeyatvAt.h | anuvR^itternityatayApAdanAnatirekAt.h | nanu bhavedevamasvarasanityasya, na svarasanityasyeti chenna, IshvarAtiriktte svarasanityatAsammateH | iyAMstu visheShaH | duritaprAgabhAvAdernityakarmAnuShThAnadvArAsmadadhInaM nityatvam.h | prakR^ityAdestvIshvarAdhInanityatvamiti bhAvaH | nanu prakR^ityAderasmadadhInanityatvam.h, kathamIshvarAdhInanityatvamiti shaN^kAparihArAyokttam.h- nityayaiveti || shaktteranyasambandhitvabhramanirAsAya svetyukttam.h | chetanA j~nAnam.h | evaMcheshvarasya mahAmahimatvena prakR^itestatsAmyAbhAvAdukttaM yukttamiti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH "pratiShedhAt.h' iti sUtravyatirikttena "tadapIteH' ityAdisUtraShaT.hkena sUchitaH | Ishvarasya mahAmahimatvAditi vadatokttaH |) || 6 || OM tAnipare tathA hyAha OM || ityatrobhayathApi sambhavena chaturmukhetaradevAH paramAtmani lIyante na veti sandehe, neti pUrvaH pakShaH, lIyanta iti siddhAntaH | tatra "paratantraH' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati-
nachAnyadevAdInAM prANAdhInatvAttatprAptiniyamAtparaprAptirnAstyeva prANaM prApya paraM devAstadanye chaiva tadgatAH | prApnuvanti paraM devaM vasanti cha yathAsukhamiti visheShashruteH || 7 || 
|| nachAnyadevAdInAmiti || anyetyataH pUrvaM prANAdapi sheShaH || prANAdhInatvAditi || chaturmukhapratibimbatvAdityarthaH | "pratibimbo hareH prANaH prANasyAnyAH kalAH smR^itAH' iti vachanAditi bhAvaH | anena paratantretyukttaparashabdaH prANavAchItyukttaM bhavati || tatprAptiniyamAditi || pratibimbasya bimbalayaniyamAditi bhAvaH | paraprAptirnAstIti | chaturmukhetaradevAnAM paramAtmapratibimbatvAbhAvAditi bhAvaH | evaMcha chaturmukhetaradevAnAM prANAkhyaparatantratayA, paramAtmani layAbhAvAjj~nAninAmapi mokShAbhAva iti neti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH prANadvArA paramAtmani layapratipAdakashrutigrAhakeNa "tathA hyAha' ityanena sarvadevAnAM prANAdhInatvena tatraiva laya iti sUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "visheShaH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM pramANodAharaNapUrvakaM 
vivR^iNoti- prANamiti || anena visheSha ityatra shrutiriti sheSha ityukttaM bhavati | tadanye devebhyo.anye R^iShyAdayaH, ata eva prAk.h devAnAmityukttam.h | anena sUtre tAnItyetadR^iShyAdyupalakShakamityukttaM veditavyam.h | prANapratibimbatvarUpaparatantratvavirodhaparihArArthamukttam.h- prANaM prApyeti || prApyaivetyevashabdasambandhaH tathAcha niyamoktayA prANapratibimbatvasya paramAtmani laye taddvAratvena gatirukttA bhavati | paraM prApnuvanti lIyanta ityarthaH | sAmAnyato.asheShajIvAnAM bhagavatpratibimbatvAditi bhAvaH | tadgatA ityanena prANasya paramAtmaprAptau prANapraviShyAnAM paramAtmaprAptiraparihAryetyukttaM bhavati | evaMcha visheShashruteH prANadvArA paramAtmaprAptisambhavAdukttaM yukttamiti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH "tathAhyAha' ityanenaivokttaH |) || 7 || OM avibhAgo vachanAt.h OM || ityatra, mukttatvena svAtantyasya bhagavaddharmatvena kiM mukttAH svatantrA na veti sandehe, svatantrA iti pUrvaH pakShaH, neti siddhAntaH | tatra "samAnadharmaH' ityukttaM vipakShabAdhakatarkatrayapUrvapakShanyAyaM tadanugrAhyahetupradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha satyasaN^kalpatvAderIshvarasaN^kalpAdyanusAritvaniyame saMsArasamAnadharmatvaM muktteriti vAchyam.h | 
|| nacha satyasaN^kalpatvAderiti || Adipadena mukttatvAdergrahaNam.h | mukttAH svatantrA iti vAkyamadhyAhAryam.h | ayamarthaH | mukttAH svatantrAH, satyasaN^kalpatvAt.h, mukttatvAt.h, Ishvaravat.h | nachAprayojako hetuH | asvAtante saMsAra iva duHkhAdiprApteH | nacha satyasaN^kalpatvamasiddham.h | "R^ite devAH' iti bhAShyodAhR^itashrutisiddhatvAt.h | nanu yachChrutyAdau satyasaN^kalpAdikamuchyate, tatparameshvarasaN^kalpAdyanusAreNaiva, na tu svAtanteNa | nacha tatsvAtante sAdhakam.h | tadabhAve.api tasyopapatterityAshaN^kA | tatra bAdhakamAha- Ishvareti || satyasaN^kalpatvAderityanuvartate | saMsArasamAnadharmatvaM syAditi sheShaH | yadi satyasaN^kalpatvAderIshvarasaN^kalpAdyanusAritvaniyamo.aN^gIkriyate, tadAtyantAsvAtantyaprAptyA duHkhAdiprAptiH syAt.h | tatashcha muktteH saMsArasamAnadharmatvaM syAt.h | na chaivam.h | ata IshvarAdyanadhInameva satyasaN^kalpatvAdikamaN^gIkAryam.h | tatashcha tasya svAtantyasAdhakatvaM sambhavatIti bhAvaH | yadvA pratij~nAhetU bahireva kR^itvA tatrAnyathAsiddhishaN^kAnirAsakatvenedaM yojyam.h | evaMcha mukttAnAmasvAtante muktteH saMsArasamAnadharmatvaprAptyA mukttAH svatantrA eveti paramAtmanaH sarvottamatvokttirviruddheti neti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH mukttau pAratante.api saMsAravaiShamyeNa duHkhAdyabhAvaM sAdhayatA "avibhAgaH' ityanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "kR^itArthatA' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- 
kR^itArthatvenaiva visheShopapatteH | apUrNatAdibhAvo vA duHkhaM vA nAsti kiJNchana | mukttasya pAratante.api tAratamye.apyataH sukhIti cha shrutiH || 8 || 
|| kR^itArthatveneti || kR^itArthatvena mukttatvena IshvarapAratante.api, mukttAnAM mukttatvAdeva duHkhAbhAvasatyasaN^kalpatvAdivisheShopapatterityarthaH | idamukttaM bhavati | yadukttam.h satyasaN^kalpatvAderIshvarasaN^kalpAdyanusAritvaniyamAN^gIkAre mukttAnAmatyantAsvAtantApattyA duHkhAdiprAptau saMsArasamAnadharmatvaM syAditi | tanna | yadA khalu bhagavadichChAnanusAreNechChati tadA tadalAbhena duHkhAdikamanubhavati | mukttAstu sarvadA bhagavadichChAnusAreNaiva kAmayante | ato bhagavatkAmanimittena mukttakAmAnantaramevakAmitaprApterasvatantrANAmapi aduHkhitvamupapannam.h | mukttasya pAratante.api duHkhaM nAstItyatra pramANamAha- apUrNatAdibhAvo veti || yato mukttAnAM pAratante.api kiJNchana duHkhaM nAsti | ato muktaH sukhI yujyate | mukttAmukttayoH paratantratvAvisheShe.api, mukttaH sarvaduHkhavinirmukttatvena sukhItyuchyate | natu saMsArIti bhAvaH | nanu mukttAnAmIshvarapAratante parasparaM sAmyasya shrutyAdiviruddhatvAttAratamyamaN^gIkartavyam.h | tatashcha parasparadveSheShyarAdinA duHkhAdiprApteH kiJNchana duHkhaM nAstIti kathamukttamityata ukttam.h- tAratamye.apyapUrNatAdibhAvo nAstIti || syAdetadevam.h | yadi mukttAnAmapUrNatAdi bhAvaH syAt.h | na chaivam.h | svasya yogyatAnusAreNa sarveShAmapi pUrNatvAtsvasyApUrtau hi tasya kAmena tadabhAvena duHkhAdiprAptiH syAt.h | saMsAriNAM tu svasyApUrNatvAdibhAvasya vidyamAnatvenAdhikakAmane duHkhAdiprAptiriti bhAvaH | evaMcha mukttasya kR^itAthartvAtpAratante.api duHkhAdyaprAptyA muktteH saMsArasamAnadharmatvAbhAvAdyukttA viShNoH sarvottamateti | (ayaM cha nyAyo "brahmamatyanukUlA' iti smR^ityanusAreNeti mukttAnAM satyakAmatvamiti bhAShyodAhR^itasmR^ityanuusAreNa cha "kAmena me kAma AgAt.h' ityekavachanatvAttadgrAhakeNa "vachanAd.h' ityanena sUchitaH |) || 8 || OM tadokograjvalanaM tatprakAshikadvAro vidyAsAmathyarAt.h OM || ityatra, maraNatvaj~nAnisambandhitvAbhyAM j~nAninAM kiM maraNaM aj~najanamaraNavadeva uta vailakShaNyeneti sandehe, aj~najanamaraNavadeveti pUrvaH pakShaH, tadvailakShaNyeneti siddhAntaH | tatra "kR^itasheShatA' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM 
tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha prArabdhakarmasheShatvAdutkrAntAvavisheSho j~nAninaH j~nAnodayAnantaraM sarvadA j~nAnaphalasyAnuvR^itteH | 
|| nacha prArabdhakamarsheShatvAditi || utkrAntau maraNe, avisheSho j~nAnibhiriti sheShaH | idamukttaM bhavati | nAj~nAnimaraNApekShayA j~nAnimaraNasya visheShaH | tasyApyanyamaraNavatprArabdhanibandhanatvAt.h | nacha tadA prArabdhAbhAvaH | tasya dehatyAgAdyavasAnatvAt.h | nacha satyapi prArabdhe vilakShaNaM j~nAnimaraNamiti yukttam.h, visheShakAraNAbhAvAditi | anena kR^itasya prArabdhakarmaNaH sheSho yasya sa tathokttastasya bhAvaH kR^itasheShateti vyadhikaraNabahuvrIhirityukttaM bhavati | anyathA talpratyayAnupapattiH | evaMcha j~nAnimaraNasyAj~namaraNasAdhAraNyAnna j~nAnasyAtishaya iti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH, "tachCheShagatyanusmR^itiyogAchcha' ityanena prArabdhakarmAvasAnasya gatyanusmR^itikAlInatvoktayA prArabdhakarmaNastaddhetukavishiShyotkramaNapratibandhakatvasUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "shashvadanupravR^ittiH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- j~nAneti || shashvadityasyArthaH sarvadeti | anvityasyArtho j~nAnodayAnantaramiti | j~nAnaphalasyeti | saJNchitakarmakShayAgAmyasheShaprArabdhopamardotkramaNAderityarthaH | ayaM bhAvaH | prArabdhakarmavattvAvisheShe.api j~nAnina utkrAntau visheSho yujyate | j~nAnasAmarthyAdeva visheShopapatteH | nacha j~nAnasyAvidyAnivR^ittimAtraphalakatvena kathamutkrAntiphalakatvamiti vAchyam.h, j~nAnasya svodayamArabhya sarvadA phalajanakatvenotkrAntyAderapi tatphalatvasambhavAt.h utkrAntermokShaikadeshatvena hatuetvopapatteshcha | tatashcha j~nAnalakShaNavisheShakAraNasadbhAvena j~nAnimaraNasyAj~namaraNavailakShaNyopapattau kR^itasheShatvamaprayojakamiti | nanu kiM prArabdhakarmasadbhAvamaN^gIkR^itya j~nAnasAmarthyenaiva vishiShyotkramaNopapAdanena | saJNchitasyeva prArabdhasyApi j~nAnenaiva vinAshamaN^gIkR^itya visheShotkramaNaM kuto nopapadyata ityAshaN^kAM pariharan.h j~nAnasya sodayamArabhya phaladatve pramANamAha- 
prArabdhakarmasheShastu virajAtaraNAvadhiH | svodayAtphaladaM j~nAnamAdehaM karma vA.a.araveH | tathApi prakR^iterbandho brahmaNA saha bhidyata iti shrutiH sharIre pApmano hitvA sarvAnkAmAn.h samashnute | 
|| prArabdhakarmeti || sodayAditi lyablopanimittA paJNchamI | sodayamArabhyetyarthaH | karma prArabdham.h, AdehamAravervA phaladamityarthaH | adhikArabhedena vyavasthitavikalyo.ayam.h | "vaishvAnare dyunadyAM vA sUyare vA deha eva vA | vidhUya sarvapApAni' ityAdipramANokttamapi grAhyam.h | atra prArabdhakarmaNaH phaladatvoktayA j~nAninAmapi tatsadbhAvo.avagamyate | nanu yadi karmA.a.adehamAravervA phaladaM, tarhi tadanantarameva liN^gabhedaH syAt.h | na chaivam.h | "brahmaNA saha bhidyate' iti vakShyamANatvena tadAnIM liN^gabhaN^gAbhAvAdityata ukttam.h- prArabdhakarmasheShastviti || na vayaM sUryAdau niHsheShaprArabdhavinAshaM brUmaH | yena pramANavirodhaH syAt.h | kiM tu sasheShameva | tachCheShastu virajAtaraNAvadhiH | tatra liN^gabhaN^gastu vartata eva | anyathA sharIrAvasthAnasya nirnibandhanatvApatteriti bhAvaH | nanu yadi j~nAnaM svodayamArabhya phaladaM, tarhi tadanantarameva liN^gabhaN^go.api syAt.h | tasyApi j~nAnaphalatvAdityata Aha- tathApIti || yadyapi j~nAnaM svodayamArabhya phaladaM, tathApItyarthaH | prArabdhakamarNa eva pratibandhakatvAditi bhAvaH | "AdehaM karma phaladam.h' ityatra spaShyaM pramANamAha- sharIra iti || AraverityatrApi, tadAha- 
satejasi sUrye sampanno yathA pAdodarastvachA vinirmuchyata evaM haiva pApmanA vinirmukttaH sa prApnoti virajAM nadIm.h | tatsukR^itaduShkR^ite vidhUnate | 
|| satejasIti || satramAtreNoN^kAreNa paramapuruShAbhidhyAtA dhyeyaM parameshvaramaparokShIkR^itya tejasi tejorUpe sUrye, sampannaH samprApnotIti yAvat.h | sUryaM prApya chAsau yathA pAdodaraH tvachA jINaryA vinirmuchyate, evaM khalu sa dhyAnI pApmanA prArabdhena vinirmuktto bhavatItyarthaH | prArabdhakarmasheShastvityatrApi pramANamAha- sa prApnotIti || tattatra sukR^itamaniShyaM sukR^itaduShkR^ite tachCheShamityarthaH | tathApi prakR^iterbandha ityatrApi pramANamAha- 
te brahmaloke tu parAntakAle parAmR^itAtvaparimuchyanti sarva iti cha | anyathAbhAvaniyamo.anR^itatAkAryakAraNa iti cha || 9 ||
|| te brahmaloka iti || ye sanyAsayogAt.h | lyablopanimittA paJNchamI | kAmyakamarparityAgalakShaNopAyaM sampAdyetyarthaH | yatayaH satkarmAnuShThAnaprayatnavantaH | ata eva shuddhaM satvamantaH karaNaM yeShAM te tathokttAH | ata eva "vedAntavij~nAnasunishchitArthAH' vedAntashravaNajanitavij~nAnena sunishchito.arthaH parabrahmarUpo yaiste tathokttAH | kAmyakarmaparityAgapUrvakasatkarmAnuShThAnenAntaHkaraNashuddhiM sampAdya sampAditamokShaj~nAnA iti yAvat.h | brahmaloke satyaloke viShNuloke vA tiShThanti te prApnuvantIti yAvat.h | te sarve.api parAntakAle chaturmukhasyAyuHparisamAptikAle parAmR^itAt.h prakR^iteH prAkR^itasyApyanR^itatvAtparetyukttam.h | parimuchyantItyarthaH | nanu prakR^itiprAkR^itayoH satyatvAtkathamanR^itatvamityata Aha- anyatheti 
|| kAryakAraNa iti dvandvaikavadbhAvaH mahattvAdikArye pradhAnAdikAraNa ityarthaH | kAryakAraNayoryAnR^itatA shrutAvuchyate | so.anyathAbhAvaniyamaH pariNAma eva | nanu mithyAtvamityarthaH | tadukttam.h | "anR^itaM pariNAmataH | prakR^itiprAkR^itaM prokttam.h' iti | evaMcha j~nAnimaraNasyAj~namaraNavilakShaNatvAdyukttaM j~nAnasya mAhAtmyamiti | (ayaM cha nyAyo "vidyAsAmarthyAt.h' ityanenaiva svotpattimArabhyaiva phaladatvarUpAparokShaj~nAnasAmarthyAditi vadatokttaH |) || 9 || OM yoginaH pratismaryate smArte chaite OM || ityatra, gatyanusmR^itI ityukttisphuTapramANAdarshanAbhyAM vidyAgatismR^itI apekShite na veti sandehe, neti pUrvaH pakShaH, apekShite iti siddhAntaH | tatra "lokopamA' ityukttaM pUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati-
nacha kR^iShyAdilaukikasAdhanasya phalasmaraNAnapekShatvAtsvargamokShayorapi tathAtvamiti vAchyam.h | 
|| nacha kR^iShyAdIti || iti sUtragatadvivachanAnurodhAtsvargetyukttam.h | evaMcha lokopamatvAdvidyAgatismR^itI nApekShite iti na j~nAnasya sampUrNamokShArthateti neti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH "smArte chaite' ityanena gatyanusmaraNAdyatirikttasAdhanasamuchchAyakachashabdena loke phalAnusmR^itivyatirikttasAdhanena phalaprApterna gatyanusmR^ityapekShAniyamaM cheti sUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "shashvadanupravR^ittiH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM pramANodAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- 
kriyAnuvR^ittirlaukike sAdhane tu mano.anuvR^ittirvaidike sAdhane syAt.h | phalaM bhavetsarvathetyeva tasmAtsmaretsadA nishchitatvena vidvAniti shrutestadanusAryanuvR^itterlaukikavaidikayoH sAmyAt.h | ato.atra phalAnusmaraNaM lavanAdikR^iShyanuvR^ittivaddR^iShyavyam.h | vachanaprAmANyAt.h || 10 || 
|| iti shrImannyAyavivaraNe chaturthAdhyAyasya dvitIyaH pAdaH || 
|| kriyAnuvR^ittiriti || sarvatheti itishabdaH prakAravachanaH | yataH kriyA manovR^ittirUpavisheShaNatyAgena sarvathAnuvR^ittyaiva phalaM bhavet.h | tasmAdvidvAn.h smaredeveti sambandhaH | lavanAdi ChedanAdi, ayaM bhAvaH | yathA khalu ChedanAdau na karShaNAdyAvR^ittiH, kiM tu parashorudyamyodyamya dAruNi nipAtAvR^ittiH | kR^iShyAdau tu nAsau, kiM tu karShaNAdyAvR^ittireva | na tAvatA lokAnanusAritA | avAntaravisheShANAM vailakShaNye.apyanuvR^ittimAtrasyobhayatra sAmyAttathA prakR^ite.api | avadhIritakriyAmanovR^ittitvavisheShasyAnuvR^ittimAtrasya laukikavaidikayoH sAdhanayoH sAmyAditi | phalasmaraNasApekShatvaM gateryukttiviruddhaM kathamaN^gIkAryamityata Aha- vachaneti || yuktterAbhAsatvAditi bhAvaH | evaMcha shashvadanuvR^ittyAnugamanasya vidyAdisApekShatvamiti j~nAnasya sampUrNamokShArthatvamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "smArte chaite' ityanenaiva manovR^ittirUpasmaraNApekShatvoktayA shashvatsadAmanaso.anuvR^ittiriti sUchanena sUchitaH |) || 10 ||
|| iti shrImannyAyavivaraNe bhAvabodhaTIkAyAM chaturthAdhyAyasya dvitIyaH pAdaH || OM brahmanADyotkrAntAnAM brahmaprAptyarthaM mArgasya tena mAgareNa gatAnAM gamyasya cha nirNAyake.asminpAde pratyadhikaraNapUrvapakShasiddhAntanyAyAH anuvyAkhyAyAmukttAH | "sukramavikramau cha sAntAnikaM prAptirabhIShyatA cha | saukaryamityanyamatasya tarkA visheShasamprAptirurutvamAptiH | kramAnurAgaH kathitAnuvR^ittiH siddhAntanirNItikarAH' iti || OM archirAdinA tatprathiteHOM || ityatra "te.archiShamabhisambhavanti yadAha puruSho.asmAllokAtpreti sa vAyumAgachChati' iti shrutyavaShyambhenArchiShaH prAthamyaM vAyorveti sandehe, ubhayorapi prAthamyamiti pUrvaH pakShaH, archiSha eva prAthamyamiti siddhAntaH | tatra "sukramaH' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati-
nacha tatratatra mArgasyAnyathoktteradhikAribhedena pR^ithaN^mArgasukramopapattiriti vAchyam.h sarve vA ete utkrAmanti te.archiShamevAbhisaMyanti tato vAyuM tatohaH pUrvapakShamityeSha u eva brahmapathaH | dve sR^itI aR^iNavaM pitR^iNAmahaM devAnAmutamartyAnAm.h | tAbhyAmidaM vishvamejatsameti yadantarA pitaraM mAtaraM cheti visheShashrutito j~nAninAmekamArgasyaiva prApteH | eSha eva brahmapatha ityavadhAraNavirodhAdanyathA |
|| nacha tatratatreti || tatra tatrodAhR^itashrutidvaye mArgasyAnyathArchirAditvena vAyvAditvena chokttatvAnmArgabhedenobhayoH prAthamikatve.apyadhikAribhedena virodhAbhAvAchcha mArganAnAtvalakShaNasukramopapattirityarthaH | evaMcha sukramopapattermArgasya nirNayAbhAvAttadanusmR^ityayoga iti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAya HarchiH prAptireva prathamenArchirAditvetyanenArchiSha eva prathamaprApyatvoktayA sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "visheShasamprAptiH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM pramANodAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- sarve vA eta iti || tato vAyumityetAvatyudAhartavye.anyAMshodAharaNamuttaratropayokShyate | anena visheShAchChrutyAdirUpA jj~nApakAdarchiH prAthamikasyaiva j~nAnikartR^ikaprApteriti nyayo vivR^ito bhavati | satyamityasyArthaH eveti | te.archiShamityasyAH shruteH kathaM visheShashrutitvamityata Aha- eSha eveti || anyathA mArgabhede, anena mArgaikyavisheShashrutitvamupapAditamiti draShyavyam.h | 
upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | mArgasyArchirAditve.api te.archiShamevetyavadhAraNayukttatvena tato vAyumiti vAyordvitIyaprApyatvapratipAdakatvena cha visheShashrutitvaM draShyavyam.h | nanu sarveShAM svargamokShaprApakadhamArchirAdimArgadvayaprAptau tamaHprabhR^ityadhogatiH keShAJNchinna syAt.h | santi cha tathAvidhAH kechit.h | ataH kathaM dve smR^itI ityatra vishvamityukttamityAshaN^kAnirAsArthaM shrutAvejadityukttamityAshayenAha- 
ejaditi vaidikAnuShThAnavata uktternAdhogativirodhaH | punarAvartino ye tu teShAM dhUmapatho dhruvaH | anyeShAmarchirAdishcha tadbhedo madhyasaMsthitiH | dhUmArchirAdidevebhyaH prApyAnuj~nAM tu madhyagAH | vihR^itya sveShyadesheShu tadUrdhvaM yAti chAdharam.h | atyalpAnAmavij~nAtApyanuj~nAvartinAM bhavet.h | puMdvAreNa svadR^iShyayA vA yathAyogyaM vimuchyatAm.h | ato na mArgabhedo.asti na hi mArgo.atra sambhavaH | pretatvaM chAdharo mArgaH pApajatvAttayoH pR^ithagiti smR^iteshcha || 1 || 2 || 3 || 4 || 
|| ejaditIti || vaidikAnuShThAnavata iti sAvadhAraNam.h, mArgadvayasyeti sheShaH | tatashchAyaM mantrArthaH | martyAnAM maraNashIlAnAM mokShasvagarAdigantR^iNAM dve eva sR^itI mArgAvihamR^iNavam.h | ke te devAnAM pitR^iNAM cha sambandhinyau devayAnapitR^iyAnalakShaNe | "dyaunarH pitA pR^ithivI mAtA' iti shruteH pitaraM mAtaraM chAntarA dyAvApR^ithivyormadhye vartamAnaM yadetatpratyavAyAdbibhyat.h vedokttapravR^ittanivR^ittakarmAdisAdhanasampUrNamaditi yAvat.h | idaM vishvaM jIvajAtaM tAbhyAM sR^itibhyAM brahma svargaM cha sametIti | anenAsyAH shruterbrahmamArgaikya eva visheShashrutitvamupapAditaM bhavati | brahmamArgasyaikatve.archirAditve cha spaShyaM smR^itiM chAha- punarAvartina iti || na "nvAtmetyeva paraM devamupAsya harimavyayam.h' ityAtmatvamAtropAsakAnAmasti tAvanmukttiH | "kechidatraiva muchyanta ityuktteH | nanveteShAM devAnAmiva svottamapraveshena dehalayadvArA mukttiH, atyalpatvAt.h | nApyutkramaNaM, "notkrAmanti' ityukttatvAt.h | nahyutkramaNashUnyAnAmarchirAdimArgaH sambhavati | "utkrAntimArgashcha vimukttagamyam.h' iti teShAmevArchirAdimArgoktteH | atasteShAM mukttermArgAntaraM vakttavyamiti kathamapunarAvartimArgaikyamityata Aha- atyalpAnAmiti || puMdvAreNa svAmitvamevopAsyamiti gurUpadeshena, "svadR^iShyayA yasya guNAH pratibhAsantyupAsane' ityukttarItyA vAnuvatirnAM svAmitvamAtropAsanAvidhibaddhAnAM yathAyogyaM vimuchyatAM svopAsanAnusAreNotkramaNamArgavyatirikttakarmakShayabhogamAtralakShaNamukttiM gachChatAm.h | ata eva chaturguNopAsakApekShayAtyalpAnAmavij~nAtApi tadokograjvalanaM tatprakAshitadvAra ityukttarItyA j~nAtabrahmanADIvyatirikttApi chakShuH shrotrAdirUpA gatirmArgo bhavedyataH, ato nArchirAdimArge.avAntarabhedo.astItyarthaH | tathokttaM bR^ihadAraNyakabhAShye, "kechittu mAnuShA mukttimanutkramyaiva dehataH | dehapAte tu dehasya doShAnmuktayaiva sarvashaH | maraNochChUnatAdInstu svakIyArabdhakarmajAt.h | dehakShINe tu gachChanti dR^iShTvA viShNumanuj~nayA | punaratraiva tiShThanti nityAnandaikabhoginaH' iti | devavyatirikttAnAmutkrAntyAdisampUrNamokShavatAmevArchirAdimArgaikyaM, na tu sarveShAmiti bhAvaH | nanu dyuparjanyAderjIvotpattimArgasya pretatvasya cha satvAt.h kathaM na mArgabheda ityata Aha- nahIti || sambhava utpattiH | tayordevayAnapitR^iyAnayoH sakAshAt.h UrdhvalokagamanamArgayorevAtra vipakShitatvAditi bhAvaH | evaMcha samprAptyA ekasyaiva mArgasya nirNayAdanusmR^itisambhavAditi bhAvaH || 1 || OM nacha vAyushabdAdavisheShavisheShAbhyAm.h OM || ityatra, "sa vAyumAgachChati archiShohaH' iti shrutyavaShyambhena vAyoraho vA dvitIyaprApyatvamiti sandehe, ubhayarorapIti pUrvaH pakShaH, vAyoreveti siddhAntaH | tatrApi sukramavisheShasamprAptirUpapUrvapakShasiddhAntanyAyAveva "nacha tatra' ityAdinA nyAyavivaraNena vivR^itau | tathA hi | tatratatra sa vAyumAgachChati, achirSho.ahariti shrutidvaye mArgasyAnyathA vAyordvitIyatvena ahno dvitIyatvena choktteriti pUrvapakShanyAyavivaraNAMshayojanA | shiShyaM pUrvavat.h | pUrvapakShanyAyashcha vAyoreva sukramopapatteriti sUchanena sUchitaH | siddhAnte tUdAhR^itya shrutyAdermAgarsyaikatve pUrvavadeva | visheSharUpatvaM vAyordvitIyatve cha tato vAyuM tato.ahariti vAyvahnoH krameNa dvitIyatR^itIyatayA prApyatvapratipAdakatvenetyapi draShyavyam.h | ekamArgasyaivetyasya cha tatrApi vAyudvitIyakasyetyarthaH | ata eva tatvaprakAshikAyAmatadadhikAribhedena mArgabhedAddvitIyaprApyatvamiti pUvarH pakShaH, na mArgabhedena dvayordvitIyaprApyatvaM kiM tveka eva mArgaH | tatrApi mArge.archiSho.anantarameva vAyuM gachChanti | nacha shrutyantaravirodhaH | vAyoranantaramahnaH prAptisambhavAditi bhAvaH iti pUrvapakShasiddhAntau darshitau | tadetadukttaM sambandhadIpikAyAM, "vAyushabdAdavisheShavisheShAbhyAM sukramo visheShasamprAptiH' iti | (siddhAntanyAyashcha, "visheShaH' ityanena bhAgena "sa ito gato dvitIyAm.h' iti visheShashrutyA vAyoreva dvitIyaprApyatvasya prApyatvAditi vadatA sUchitaH |) || 2 || OM taTito.adhivaruNaH sambandhAt.h OM || ityatra, "saMvatsarAdvaruNalokaM saMvatsarAttaTitam.h' iti shrutyavaShyambhena saMvatsarAnantaraM varuNalokasya prApyatvamuta taTita iti sandehe, ubhayorapIti pUvarH pakShaH, taTita eveti siddhAntaH | tatrApi sukramavisheShaprAptirUpAmeva pUrvapakShasiddhAntanyAyau "nacha tatra' ityAdinA nyAyavivaraNenaiva vivR^itau | tathAhi | tatratatra saMvatsarAdvaruNalokaM saMvatsarAttaTitamiti shrutidvaye mArgasyAnyathA taTillokasya varuNalokasya || nacha somAdagnimiti || pradhAnavAyorapItyapishabdaH pradhAnatvasya prayojakatvaj~nApanArthashcha anena mArge.adhamaprAptyanantaramuttamasyaiva prAptirityuttamatvakramAnusAreNa prAptikramAbhAva iti chottamasomendrAdiprAptyanantaramagnidhruvaprAptyottamakramApekShayA viparItakrama iti vA vikrama ityetadvivR^itaM bhavati | evaMcha vikramAnmukhyavAyorapyanantaramanyasya prApyatvasambhavAnna tasyAtishayena prAdhAnyamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyo "vaidyutenaiva tat.h' ityanena vidyutpatinA vAyunaiva brahma gachChatIti vadatA uttamatvakramaviparItakrameNa prApyatvashravaNAnmukhyavAyoranantaraM anyaH prApyo.astIti sUchanena sUchitaH | ) taddhetutvena "urutvam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti | uttamatvAditi || tasyaivetyetadubhayatrApi sambaddhayate | anenAntimaprApyatvasAdhakabrahmaprApayitR^itvashakttisAdhakatvena paramparayA vAyorantimaprApyatvasAdhakamurutvamityukttaM bhavati | brahmaprApayitR^itvashaktterasiddhiM parihartuM shrutimudAharati- vAyureveti || pUrvapakShayuktteranyathAsiddhimAha-

|| mArgetviti || nanu vAyoranantaraM brahmapriyasyaiva prApyatvAbhyupagame tasyApi brahmaprApayitR^itvasambhava ityata Aha- nahi rAjAnamiti || vAyoreva tu brahmAtipriyatvaM brahmaprApayitR^itvaM cha klR^iptamiti bhAvaH | evaMchorutvAdvAyoreva brahmaprApayitR^itvamiti yukttaM tasya prAdhAnyamiti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH "tachChrutaH' ityanena vAyoruttamatvapratipAdakashrutigrAhakeNa sUchitaH |) || 5 || OM kAryaM bAdarirasya gatyupapatteH OM || ityatra, "sa etAn.h brahma gamayati' iti shrutyukttabrahmashabdashravaNAtkiM mukhyaM vA utAmukhyamutobhayamityatrApyekasyobhayaprApyatvasambhavAtkashchitparaM kashchitkAryamityarthaH syAt.h | tatra kiM kenachitkrameNobhayaprAptiruta kramaM vinaiva svechChAnusAreNa, kramapakShe.api kiM kashchidyogyatArUpaH kramastadanyo veti sandehe, kAryameva parameva kramaM vinA svechChAnusAreNobhayaprAptiH, kramapakShe.api yogyatAtiriktta eva krama iti pUrvaH pakShaH, ubhayamapi shrutyukttaM kenachitkrameNaivobhayaprAptistatrApi yogyatArUpa eva krama iti siddhAntaH | tatra kAryameveti prathamapakShe "sAntAnikam.h' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAmarthAttatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati-

|| nacha chaturmukheti || santatatvAdbandhasyeti | "tathApi prakR^iterbandho brahmaNA bhidyate' iti vachanAditi bhAvaH | bhagavatprAptirnAstIti kintu chaturmukhaprAptireveti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH, "asya gatyupapatteH' ityanena chaturmukhamukttiparyantaM santatatvAdbandhasya pralayAtpUrvaM kAryasyaiva gatyupapatteriti vadatA sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "AptiH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM pramANodAharaNapUvarkaM vivR^iNoti- yAnti devamiti || kechidapratIkAlambanAH, paraM kechitpratIkAlambanAH vibhuM chaturmukhaM, laye layAtpUrvaM, yAntItyarthaH | ayamubhayaprAptirUpo visheShaH yogyatAtAratamyarUpakrameNaiveShyate, natu yatheShyamityarthaH | yAnti devamiti pUrvArdhasyaivAtropayoge.apyuttarArdhodAharaNaM tu yogyatArUpakrameNaivobhayAprAptiriti vakShyamANachaturthasiddhAntapakShayeti j~nAtavyam.h | (ayaMcha nyAyo.apratIkAlambanAnnayatItyenApratIkAlambanAt.h paraM nayati, pratIkAlambanAtkAryaM nayatItyuktayA "yAnti devam.h' iti pramANabalenobhayaprApteH prAptatvAditi sUchanena sUchitaH |) paramevetyasminpUrvapakShe "prAptiH' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati-
