|| nacha parabrahmaNa iti || prathamaprAptatvAditi | mukhyAmukhyayormukhya eva sampratyayAditi bhAvaH | apohAyuktterbAdhakAbhAvAditi bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "paraM jaiminirmukhyatvAt.h' ityanena brahmashabdasya parabrahmaNyeva mukhyatA brahmashabdena tasyaiva prApteriti sUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena, "AptiH' ityukttameva siddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- yAnti devamiti || atra kAryameva parameveti pUrvapakShadvaye ubhayamityeka eva siddhAnta iti anuvyAkhyAne prAptirityeka eva siddhAntanyAya ukttaH | atrApi yAnti devamiti pramANodAharaNenaika eva nyAyaH pUrvapakShadvayanirAsakatvena dvivAraM vivR^itaH | ata eva prAgukttanyAyAdeveti sUchayituM prAptatvAdevetyevashabdaH | (ayaMcha nyAyo.apratIkAlambanAnnayatItyanena kAryaparayorubhayorapi prApteH pramANabalena prAptatvAditi sUchanena sUchitaH |) kramaM vinA svechChAnusAreNaivobhayaprAptiriti tR^itIyapakShe, "abhIShyatA' ityukttaM pUrvapakShanyAyaM 
kiJNchidvivR^iNvanpratikShipati- nacha paraprAptiriti || tatprAptirityanantaraM yasya chaturmukhaprAptirabhIShyA, tasya tatprAptirityapi grAhyam.h | ubhayatrApi sAdhakasadbhAvAt.h | "yatprAptumabhivAJNChanti' ityAdivachanAchcha kramasya chAdarshanAditi bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "tatkratuH' ityanena tatprAptIchChAmAtreNa tatprAptiniShedhapUrvakaM kramAbhidhAyikAyAH "sa yathA kAmo bhavati' iti shruteH grAhakeNa sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "kramAnurAgaH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM pramANodAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti-
kramAnurAgI bhagavAnkramAtpumbhiravApyate | ataH kramAtsamR^iddhe tu j~nAne brahmalaye naraiH | prApyante niyamenaiva kaishchidevApyate mR^itAviti bhagavataH kramAnurAgitvashruteH | nacha bahudhAshruteryathAsaukaryaM chaturmukhasya parasya vA prAptiriti vAchyam.h shrutyukttAnuvR^ittereva nyAyyatvAt.h | sampratIkAshchaturmukhamapratIkAH paramamuhate gachChantyAgachChanti cha chatuurmukhAtparamaM parAchchaturmukhaM yAvadvilayamatha saha chaturmukhena vimuchyante Anandino bhavatIti hi shrutiH | antarbhedAdhikaraNatvAtsamudAyokttiH || 5 || 6 || 
|| iti shrImannyAyavivaraNe chatutharAdhyAyasya tR^itIyaH pAdaH || 
|| kramAnurAgIti || naraiH pratIkAlambanaiH, chaturmukhaprAptipUrvakaM prApyate | kaishchidapratIkAlambanaiH, sAkShAdApyata ityatra bhagavAnityanuvartate | mR^itAviti, layAtpUrvamityarthaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH "tatkratushcha' ityanena sUchitaH |) kramapakShe.api yogyatAtirikttaH saukaryarUpa eva krama iti pUrvapakShe, "saukaryam.h' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- nacha bahudheti || pakShadvayasyApi prAmANikatvenAparihAryatvAt.h | mahAphale kramAbhAvasyAyogAt.h | saukaryavyatirikttakramasya chAdarshanAditi bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "apratIkAlambanam.h' ityanena pratIkAlambanApratIkAlambanatvarUpayogyatArUpakramoktayA yasya yatprAptau saukaryaM tasya tatprAptiriti sUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "kathitAnuvR^ittiH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- shrutyuktteti || anuvR^ittiranusaraNam.h | tAmeva shrutimudAharati- sapratIkAshcheti || paramAchchaturmukhaM, chaturmukhAtparamityanvayaH | nanu "kAryaM bAdariH' ityAdidashasUtyA ekAdhikaraNatve "sAntAnikam.h' ityAdipUrvottaranyAyabAhulyaM kathamityata Aha- antarbhedeti || antarbhedo yasmin.h tadantarbhedaM, tachcha tadadhikaraNaM cha tadantabharedAdhikaraNam.h | dashasUtyA ekAdhikaraNatve bhinnAbhinnArthapratipAdanapUrvakaM gamyalakShaNaikArthapratipAdakatvenAntarbhedAdhikaraNatvAt.h "sAntAnikam.h' ityAdipUrvottarapakShanyAyasamudAyasyAvAntarapratipAdyapekShayA ukttirityarthaH | tadukttaM sambandhadIpikAyAm.h, "mArgeNAnena kiM gamyamityasyaiva vinirNaye "kAyarM bAdariH' ityAdisUtrANAM vyApR^itiryataH "kAryaprAptau na niyamaH paraprAptau cha nAsti saH | na chechChayAsya niyamo na chAniyama iShyate' ityAdirUpeNa tathA, "bahavo nirNayAshcha yat.h | antarbhedAdhikaraNamityeva tata uchyate' iti | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "apratIkAlambanAt.h' ityanenaiva sapratIkAlambanAshchatumarukhaM gachChanti shrutikathitasyaivAnusaraNIyatvAditi sUchanena sUchitaH |) || 5-6 || || iti shrImannyAyavivaraNabhAvabodhe chaturthAdhyAyasya tR^itIyaH pAdaH || 
bhogapratipAdakaitatpAdAntargatAdhikaraNapUrvapakShasiddhAntanyAyA anuvyAkhyAyAM saN^graheNoktAH | "atikramokttiH kR^itiratharlAbhaH parA gatiH pAragatistadokaH | samastakAryaM vashitA cha vishvasambhAvanAyukttayastvanyapakShe | sAmAnyarUpaM pratibhAnamukttirAshcharyatA kR^itrimatAstadoShaH | visheShaklR^iptiH kR^itanishchayashcha mAhAtmyamityeva sunirNayArthAH' iti | OM sampadyAvihAyastvena shabdAt.h OM || ityatrArchirAdyatikramoktayA brahmaNo gamyatvoktyA cha j~nAnI kiM brahmAtikramya bhogAn.h bhuN^.hkte, atha tatsamIpa eveti sandehe, atikramyaiveti pUrvaH pakShaH, samIpa eveti siddhAntaH | tatra, "atikramokttiH' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvan.h pratikShipati- 
nachainaM setuM tIrtvetyatrAtikramokttermuktto brahma tItvarAgachChati taratIti sAmAnyapratIte brahmatIrtvedaM gachChatIti visheShayuktteH | imAM ghorAmashivAM nadIM tIrtvA brahma sampadyate iti visheShoktteshchaitaM setuM pratyanyattIrtvetyanyathopapatteH || 1 ||
|| nachaitaM setumiti || atikramasyetyataH pUrvaM brahmetyupaskartavyam.h | brahmaNo.apyatikrame gamyenAnyena bhavitavyamityAshayena bhavitavyamityAshayena gachChatItyukttam.h | nanu shrutau samAnakartR^ikakriyApradarshanArthaM bhavatIti shrUyate | ata evedaM gachChatIti vakShyati | evaM chaitaM setumiti brahmaNo.apyatikramoktterna tadgamyamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH, "avihAya' ityanena brahmaNo.atikramAbhAvoktayA sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "sAmAnyarUpam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- taratIti || tIrtvetyasyArthato grahaNamidam.h | kathamanena sAmAnyapratItirityata Aha- brahma tIrtveti || tarhyanirNaya ityata Aha- etaM setuM pratIti || "setushchApi vidhAraNAt.h | sitamasmin.h jagatsarvamiti seturitIritaH | evaM setuM prati pumAnanyattIrtvA hyadoShavAn.h' ityukttashcheti bhAvaH | evaM chaitaM setumiti shruteH sAmAnyarUpatvAdetaM setuM prati anyattIrtvetyarthopapatteryukttaM tasya gamyatvamiti 
bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "shabdAd.h' ityanena "imAN^ghorAm.h' iti shrutigrAhakeNa etaM setuM tIrtvA idaM gachChatIti vachanAbhAvena sAmAnyarUpatvAdimAM ghorAmiti shrutyanusAreNa etaM setuM pratyutAnyattIrtvetyarthopapatteriti sUchanena sUchitaH |) || 1 || OM mukaH pratij~nAnAt.h OM || ityatra, "sa tatra paryeti' ityAdinAsya kriyApratIteH shrutyuktterubhayathApi sambhavAt.h kiM muktto muktto naveti sandehe, na muktta iti pUrvaH pakShaH, muktta iti siddhAntaH | tatra "kR^itiH' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha kR^itrimatvAdamuktta evochyate sa tatra paryetItyAdau svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyata iti mukttasya spaShyaM pratibhAtattvAchChrutau | sa tatra paryetIti shrutyaikyapratIteshchaivambhUtasyApi prakaraNatvaM prakalpya shrutibAdhAN^gIkAre sA shrutirapyevaM vibhajya kiM yojayituM na shakyata iti shruterevAbhAvaprasaN^gaH | satyaM j~nAnamityAdAvapi satyamityasyAnnamityanenAnvaya ityAdiprasaN^gAt.h || 2 || 
|| nacha kR^itrimatvAditi || kR^itiratra kriyA grAhyA | paryetIti shrutyAnuguNyAt.h | ata eva tatvaprakAshikAyAM, "sa tatra paryetItyAdinAsya kriyApratIteH' ityukttam.h | nacha kR^itrimatve.api mukttatvaM kiM na syAditi vAchyam.h, nahi kriyAvattvaM kR^itakR^ityasya mukttasyopapadyata iti mukttatve kriyAvattvameva na syAditi bhAvaH | evaMcha kR^itrimatvAchChrutyukttasyAmukttatvena mukttasya bhogAsambhava iti neti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH, "tatra paryeti' itishrutyukttasya mukttatvasya vidhAyakena muktta ityanena sa tatra paryetIti kriyAvattvavidhAnAdamuktta eva sarvatrochyata iti sUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "pratibhAnam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- svena rUpeNeti || iti shrutAvityanvayaH | yadveti pUrvavAkyena | shrutau sa tatra paryetItyasyAmityarthaH | nanu sa eSha samprasUto.asmAchCharIrAtsamutthAya paraJNjyotirupasampadya svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyata iti nirguNabrahmopAsakasya svarUpAvirbhAvAbhidhAyakamidaM prakaraNAntaram.h | sa tatra paryetItyatra tu pUrvokttasaguNapratipAdakadaharavidyopAsako bhogavattvenochyate, sa chAmuktta eva | tathA paraJNjyotirityasya sa tatra paryetItyasmAdbhinnaprakaraNatvAtkathamanena vAkyena tadvAkyokttabhogavataH spaShyatayA pratibhAnamityata Aha- sa tatreti || sa tatra paryetItyasya paraJNjyotiriti pUrvashrutyaikyasyaikaviShayatvasya pratIterityarthaH | "svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate sa uttamaH puruShaH sa tatra paryeti' ityAnupUrvIvishiShyavAkye sa iti tachChabdena svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyata ityukttAvirbhUtasvarUpamukttasyaiva parAmarshaH | natu dUrokttadaharavidyopAsakasya | avyavahitaparAmarshasambhave vyavahitaparAmarshakalpakAbhAvAditi bhAvaH | pratItaparityAgenAnyathAkalpane bAdhakamAha- evambhUtasyApIti || ekavAkyatayA pratItasyApi prakaraNatvaM bhinnaprakaraNatvam.h | shrutibAdhaH sa tatretyasya mukttaparatvApahAraH | sA shrutiH paraJNjyotiriti shrutiH | vibhajya paraJNjyotistiShThatItyAdirUpeNa | shrutireva ekasminnarthe pramANatayA ekavAkyatApannashruterevetyarthaH | tatashchAvyavahitatvenaikavAkyatayA pratItasyApi j~nApakaM vinA bhinnaprakaraNatvakalpane ekavAkyatayA sampratipannasya paraJNjyotirupasampadyetyasyApi tiShThatItyAdipadAdhyAhAreNa bhinnaprakaraNatvaM kalpayituM shakyata iti shrutau kiJNchidapyekArthatayaikaM vAkyaM prakaraNamiti na syAditi bhAvaH | nanu "satyaM j~nAnamanantaM brahma' ityAdishrutInAM satyAdipadAnAM brahmapadenaikArthapratipAdakatayA sAmAnAdhikaraNyarUpAnvayasambhavenaikavAkyatApannAnAM vidyamAnatvAtkathamanekavAkyatApannashruterevAbhAvaprasaN^ga ityata Aha- satyamiti || na kevalaM sA shrutireva vibhajya yojayituM shakyate, kintu satyaM j~nAnamityatrApi | evaM vyavahitAN^gIkAreNa yojanA kataruM shakyata ityaperarthaH | anena sa tatretyasya sannihitamukttaparatvatyAgena vyavahitasaguNopAsakasya jIvanmukttipratipAdakatvAN^gIkAre chAtiprasaN^ga uktto bhavati | tathA hi | annamayAdiprakaraNasya satyaM j~nAnamiti mantravarNokttapravachanarUpatvena, satyamityasya "ye.annaM brahmopAsate' ityukttAnnamityanenaikArthaprAtipAdakatvena sAmAnAdhikaraNyarUpAnvayaH syAt.h | Adipadena j~nAnamityasya, mana ityanena chAnantamityasya, AnandamityanenokttarItyA sAmAnAdhikaraNyarUpAnvayaH syAt.h | nachedaM tasyeShyam.h | satyaM j~nAnamiti mantrasyAkhaNDArthaniShThatayA brahmaparatvenAnnamayAdiprakaraNAnAM cha koshaparatvena bhinnaprakaraNatvAN^gIkArAditi pararItyaivedamApAdanaM draShyavyam.h | siddhAnte tvekaprakaraNatvasyAchAryaireva "mAntravarNikameva cha gIyate' iti sUtrArthatayopapAditatvAditi | evaMcha sa tatra paryetIti shrutyukttasya spaShyaM mukttatvapratibhAnAdyuktto mukttasya bhoga iti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "pratij~nAnAd.h' ityanena sUchitaH |) || 2 || OM AtmA prakaraNAt.h OM || ityatra, paraJNjyotirupasampadya sveneti shrutyukttajyotiHshabdavAchyatvAvisheShAtkiM viShNurAdityo veti sandehe, Aditya iti pUrvaH pakShaH, viShNuriti siddhAntaH | tatra "arthalAbhaH' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha paraJNjyotiH shabdenAdityajyotiraN^gIkAre sa tejasi sUyare sampanno yathA pAdoharastvachA vinirmuchyata evaM haiva sa pApmanA 
vinirmuktta ityAdinaikArthateti prayojanaM atha kimuchyate paraJNjyotirityAtmaiva paraJNjyotiH 
|| nacha paramiti || ekArtheti || sa tejasIti shrutisamAkhyAnAt.h AdityAkhyaM paraJNjyotirupasampadya svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate prArabdhakarmaNA muchyata ityatharsya paraJNjyotiriti vAkyasya vakttuM shakyatvAditi bhAvaH | evaMcha paraJNjyotiHshabdasyAdityaparatvAN^gIkAre sa tejasIti shrutyaikavAkyatvarUpArthalAbhAnna mukttasya brahmasamIpe bhoga iti neti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyo bhAShyAnusAreNa sAvadhAraNena hetyanena paraJNjyotiHshabdena sUrya evochyata iti sUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "ukttiH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM shrutyudAharaNapUvarkaM vivR^iNoti- ateti || paraJNjyotiHshabdavAchyatvaM kuta ityata ukttam.h - 
sahi paramo dyotate jIvAchchAjIvAchcha tasmAdAhuH paraJNjyotiriti tamevaiSha jIvo.abhisampadya svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyata iti tasyaiva paraJNjyotiShTvoktteH | sAvakAshaliN^gAnniravakAshashrutereva balavattvAt.h || 3 || 
|| sahIti || dyotate prakAshate | jyotiHshabdasyApi prakAshArthatvAditi bhAvaH | jIvAt.h brahmabhavAdeH, ajIvAt.h shrItatvAt.h, jaDaprakR^ityAdeshcha parama ityanena sambandhaH | nigamayati- tasmAditi || yadvA hi yasmAttasmAtparaM jyotirityAhuH ityanvayaH | paraJNjyotiriti paraJNjyotiriti paraJNjyotiHshabdavAchyamAtmAnamityarthaH | tamAtmAnam.h | tasyaiveti | shrutAvAtmaimevatyavadhAraNAditi bhAvaH | tarhyekArthateti liN^gasya kA gatirityata Aha- sAvakAsheti || liN^gAtsamAkhyAlakShaNAdityarthaH | tasya sAvakAshatvaM nAma paraJNjyotiriti vAkyasya sa tejasIti vAkyasamAnArthatvAN^gIkAre.api sa tejasIti vAkyasyAnupapattyabhAvaH | ubhayorabhinnArthatvasambhavAt.h shruterevetyevakAreNa jAtyApi balavattvamAchaShye | evaMcha paraJNjyotiHshabdena brahmaNa evoktterbrahma prApyaiva bhogAn.h bhuN^ktta iti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "prakaraNAt.h' ityanenAnyaprakaraNenyasyApyukttisambhavAnna prakaraNamAtreNa nirNaya iti niravakAshA paraJNjyotiHshrutirapi vivakShitA | tathAcha paraJNjyotiHshabdena paramAtmana evokttatvAnna sUryaH paraJNjyotiHshabdenoktta iti sUchanena sUchitaH |) || 3 || OM avibhAgena dR^iShyatvAt.h OM || ityatrobhayathApi sambhavAtsAyujyabhAgbhiH kiM paramAtmabhukttA eva bhogA bhujyante, uta tadabhukttA iti sandehe, tadabhukttA iti pUrvaH pakShaH, paramAtmabhukttA eveti siddhAntaH | tatra, "parA gatiH' ityukttanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha paramagatitvAdIshvarAbhukttA api bhogA mukttau bhavanti | Ishvarasya svata eva pUrNAnandatvAdabhogasyApi sambhavAditi vAchyam.h | pUrNAnandaH pUrNabhukpUrNakartA pUrNaj~nAnaH pUrNabhAH pUrNashakttiH | (pUrNaishvaryA) AshcharyatvAdbhagavAnvAsudevoviruddhashakttirnacha doShaspR^igIshaH iti shrutyAshcharyatayaiva brahmaNa ubhayoktteH | sAvakAshopapattimAtrAnniravakAshashrutiyukttopapattereva balavattvAt.h || 4 || 
|| nacha paramagatitvAditi || paramagatitvasyAprayojakatvaparihArArthamukttam.h- Ishvarasyeti || paramAtmabhukttA eva mukttau bhujyanta iti niyame, Ishvarasya nityapUrNAnandatvena kadAchidabhogasyApi sambhave tadA saJNjAtabhogechChAnAmapi mukttAnAM bhogAbhAvaprasaN^gena mokShasyApuruShArthatvApattyA paramagatitvameve na syAditi bhAvaH | evaMcha mokShasya paramagatitvAnmukttena paramAtmAbhukttA eva bhogA bhujyanta iti na tasya sarvabhokttR^itvamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH sUtrasyApUrNatvAtpUrvasUtrAdanuvR^ittena muktto vibhAgena bhogAn.h bhuN^ktta iti sambaddhena muktta ityanena muktteH paramagatitvamiti sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena, "AshcharyatA' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM shrutyudAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- pUrNAnanda iti || ubhayoktteH pUrNAnandatvapUrNabhukttatvarUpobhayoktterityarthaH | tathAcha brahmaNaH pUrNAnandatve.api, pUrNabhugiti pUrNabhogasyApi shravaNAtkadApi tasyAbhogAbhAvena saJNjAtabhogechChAnAM bhogasyaiva sambhavena yukttaM paramAtmabhukttabhogabhokttR^itvaM mukttAnAmiti bhAvaH | nanu paramagatitvayukttestarkasahitatvena prabalatvAtkathamupapattimAtrasiddhAntanirNaya ityata Aha- sAvakAsheti || paramagatitvasya mukttAnAmIshvarAbhukttabhogabhokttR^itvAbhAve.api, AvR^ittishUnyatvAdinopapatterityarthaH || shrutiyuktteti || tathA bahutvenApi prAbalyamiti bhAvaH | evaMcha brahmaNa Ashcharyatayaiva pUrNAnandatve.api pUrNabhogashravaNAdyukttaM mukttAnAM bhagavadbhukttabhogabhokttR^itvamiti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyo nyAyavivaraNAnusAreNa viruddhashakttirityAshcharyatayA pUrNAnandasyApi pUrNabhogasya dR^iShyatvAdityarthakena "dR^iShyatvAdityanena sUchitaH |) || 4 || OM brAhmeNa jaiminirupanyAsAdibhyaH OM || ityatra, vAdivipratipattyA mukttAnAM bhogo yuktto naveti sandehe, na yukta iti pUrvaH pakShaH, yuktta iti siddhAntaH | tatra, "pAragatiH' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha pAraN^gatatvAnmukttasya chinmAtradeho.api nAstIti vAchyam.h akR^itrimatvAttasya dehasyAnapagamAt.h | atha vimukttasya chinmAtra eva deho bhavati chinmAtrANi karaNAni tairIshAnugR^ihItairbhogAn.h bhuN^kte iti shruteH || 5 || 
|| nacha pAraN^gatatvAditi || pAretyataH pUrvaM saMsAreti draShyavyam.h | deho.apItyapishabdaH jaDadehAbhAvasamuchchaye kaimutye vA | nachAprayojako hetuH, dehavattve mukttatvasyaivAyogAditi bhAvaH | nacha mukttasya dehAbhAve.api na doSha iti vAchyam.h, bhogAsambhave puruShArthatvameva na syAditi | evaMcha saMsArapAragatatvena mukttasya sharIrAbhAvena bhogAsambhavAdapuruShArthatvaM muktteriti neti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH "evamapyupanyAsAt.h' ityanena, "sa eSha etasmAnyartyAt.h' iti mukttatvapratipAdakashrutisUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "akR^itrimatA' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- akR^itrimatvAditi || dehasya chinmAtrasyetyarthaH | dehasyetyasya pUrvatrottaratra cha sambandhaH | ayaM bhAvaH | chinmAtrasya jIvasvarUpasyAkR^ittimatvAt.h | kR^itrimadehasyaiva saMsArApAdakatvAdakR^itrimachinmAtradehAN^gIkAre.api na saMsArapAragatatvarUpamukttatvAnupapattiriti | mukttasya chinmAtradehAdisadbhAve shrutimAha- atheti || phalasambandhaH sphuTaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "tadAtmakatvAt.h' ityanena chinmAtradehasya mukttasvarUpatvenAkR^itrimatvAt.h chinmAtradehena bhogaH sambhavatIti sUchanena sUchitaH |) || 5 || OM saN^kalpAdeva cha tachChruteH OM || ityatra, lokadR^iShyayalaukikatvAbhyAM mukttabhogaH kiM tattadupAyasAdhyasAdhanasAdhya uta saN^kalpamAtrasAdhya iti sandehe, tattadupAyasAdhyasAdhanasAdhya iti pUrvaH pakShaH, saN^kalpamAtrasAdhya iti siddhAntaH | tatra "tadokaH' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
bhagavadokasi sthitatvAnmukttasya tasyApyokastvasAmyena tattadupAyasAdhyabhogasAdhanaM vAchyam.h | nirdoShatvAttadokaso mukttasya cha saN^kalpAdeveti shrutyanusAreNopapatteH || 6 || 
|| nacha bhagavadokasIti || tasyApi bhagavadokaso.api, okastvasyAprayojakatvashaN^kAnirAsArthamukttam.h- okastvasAmyeneti || bhUmyAdyokasetyarthaH | anyathA lokavirodhApAtAditi bhAvaH | bhagavadokasya evaMvidhatve.api, mukttabhogasya tattadupAyasAdhyasAdhanasAdhyatve, kimAyAtamityata ukttam.h- bhagavadokasi sthitatvAnmukttasyeti || tattadupAyasAdhyaM bhogasAdhanaM yasya mukttasyeti vigrahaH | evaMcha muktterapi saMsArasamAnadharmatvAdapuruShArthatvamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH, bhagavadokasa okastvasAmyAnmukttigatasya bhogo.aprayatnApekSha iti vipakShavyAvartakena cha shabdena sUchitaH | tadukttaM tatvaprakAshikAyAm.h, "chashabdo vipakShavyAvartakatayA vyAkhyAtam.h' iti |) taddhetutvena "astadoShaH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM apekShitAMshapUraNena vivR^iNoti- nirdoShatvAditi || tadokaso bhagavadokasaH, tathAcha bhagavadokastvasAmye.api bhagavadokaso lokavirodhasyaivAyukttatvAnmukttau bhogasya saN^kalpamAtrasAdhyatvAN^gIkAre na lokavirodho bAdhaka iti bhAvaH | bAdhakAbhAvamAtreNa nArthasiddhirityataH sAdhakamAha- saN^kalpAdeveti || sa yadi pitR^ilokakAmo bhavati, saN^kalpAdevAsya pitaraH samuttiShThantIti shrutyukttAnusAreNa saN^kalpamAtrasAdhyabhogavattvasyopapatterityarthaH | evaMcha bhagavadokaso nirdoShatvAnmukttabhogasya saN^kalpamAtrasAdhyatvamiti yukttaM tasya puruShArthatvamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "saN^kalpAdeva' ityanena bhagavadokasaH sadoShatve, tatprAptasya mukttasya saN^kalpAdeva kAmitaprAptirna sambhavatIti sUchanena sUchitaH |) || 6 || OM ata eva chAnanyAdhipatiH OM || ityatrobhayathApi sambhavAnmukttaH klR^iptapatibhyo.anyapatiyuktto na veti sandehe, mukttasyAdhamA api patayaH santIti pUrvaH pakShaH, na santIti siddhAntaH | tatra "tadokaH' ityukttameva pUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- nacha paragR^ihagatatvAdasya rAjagR^ihagatasyeva svAdhamA api kadAchidIshate nirdoShatvAdeva mukttasyeshvarasya tatrasthAnAM mukttAntarANAM cha rAjadoShavaddoShAsambhavAdyathAyogyameva svIkAropapatteH | 
|| nacha paragR^ihagatatvAditi || aprayojakatvashaN^kAparihArArthamukttam.h- rAjagR^ihasyeveti || anyathA lokavirodhaH syAditi bhAvaH | evaMcha tadokasi sthitatvAnmukttAvadhamA api patayaH santIti muktteH saMsArasamAnadharmatvAdapuruShArthatvamiti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAya rAjagR^ihagatasyeva bhagavadokagatasyApi mukttasya sAdhamaniyamyatvamiti vipakShavyAvartakena cha shabdena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "astadoShaH' ityukttameva siddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- nirdoShatvAdeveti || mukttasya niyamyasya | Ishvarasya prayojakasya mukttAntarANAM prayojyAnAM cha | rAjeti tadgR^ihaM gatasya pratihArAdInAM chopalakShaNam.h | rAjagR^ihagatasya svAdhamaniyamyatvaM rAjAdInAM doShavattvAdyukttam.h | atra bhagavadokogatamukttasya sarvaniyAmakeshvarasya mukttAntarANAM cha satyasaN^kalpatvena nirastAj~nAnaviruddhakAmAdidoShavattvAdeva yathAyogyamevAdhamottamabhAvAnatikrameNaiva niyamyaniyAmakabhAvasvIkAropapatteriti bhAvaH | nanu nirdoShatve pramANamAha- 
mukttAnAM patayo devA devAnAM cha prajApatiH | tasya viShNurnachaivedaM pArAvaryaM vinashyatIti shruteH || 7 || 
|| mukttAnAmiti || evaMcha bhagavadokagatatve.api mukttasya nirdoShatvAdadhamaniyamyatvAbhAvAdyukttaM muktteH puuruShArthatvamiti 
bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "ata eva' ityanena satyasaN^kalpatvAdeva svAdhamaniyamyatvaM neti vadatA IshvarAdeH sadoShatve satyasaN^kalpatvameva na syAditi sUchanena sUchitaH |) || 7 || OM abhAvaM bAdarirAha hyevam.h OM || ityatra, vAdivipratipattyA bhogo yujyate na veti sandehe neti pUrvaH pakShaH, yujyata iti siddhAntaH | tatra "samastakAyarm.h' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha dehabhAve tatkAryaduHkhAdistadabhAve bhogAsambhava iti doShaH dehAbhAvAchcha bhAvAchcha nirbhogitvaM cha duHkhitAm.h | yAntyamukttA nobhayaM cha mukttAnAM vashitA yata iti shruttyaiva visheShaklR^ipteH || 8 || 
|| nacha dehabhAva iti || dehino duHkhAdiniyamadarshanAditi bhAvaH |  abhimAnasAhityenetyapi draShyavyam.h | tena na suptyAdau vyabhichAraH | nacha dehavattvamaprayojakam.h | "na ha vai(sa)sharIrasya sataH priyApriyayorapahatirasti' iti shrutyanugR^ihItatvAt.h | tarhi mAstu deha ityata Aha- tadabhAva iti || deharahitasya bhogAdarshanAditi bhAvaH | nacha chichCharIrabrahmadehAbhyAM bhogaH samarthita eveti vAchyam.h, chichCharIrasya suptyAdau vidyamAnasyApi bhogAyatanatvAdarshanAt.h | brAhmeNa dehena sAyujyabhAjAM bhagavatpraveshadashAyAmeva gR^ihavadupapattAvapi tadanyeShAmanupapatterityadhikAshaN^kAyA pratyavasthAnAditi bhAvaH | evaMcha mukttasya dehAbhAve bhogAsambhavAddehasadbhAve tatprayukttasamastakAryaprAptyA mokShe duHkhAsambhinnasukhAprAptyApuruShAthartvamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "pradIpavadAveshaH' ityanena yathA pradIpo dIpikAdiShu praviShyastatratyaM tailameva bhuN^kte, na tu kArShNyAdi, tadvanmukttasya dehasambandhe.api sukhameva bhuN^kte, na duHkhamiti duHkhAdyabhAvaprAptiM samarthayatA sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "visheShaklR^iptiH' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM pramANodAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- dehAbhAvAchcheti || AdyadvitIyachashabdAvitaretarasamuchchaye | pralayAdAviti sheShaH | duHkhitAM cheti chashabdasambandhaH | dehAbhAvAchchetyAdenirbhogitvamityAdinA yathAkramaM sambandhaH | mukttastu nirbhogitvaM duHkhitvaM cha na yAtyevetyevArthakachaturthachashabdasambandhaH | mukttAnAM dehasadbhAvena nirbhogitvAsambhave.api duHkhaM syAdityata Aha- mukttAnAmiti || vashitA vashyakR^ititetyarthaH | tathAcha mukttasya vashyaprakR^itivashatvAbhAvAdvashyavahnayAdipuruShasya tadyogajanyaduHkhAbhAvavanmukttasya bAhyadehAN^gIkAro.api duHkhAbhAvopapattirityarthaH | evaMcha shrutyaiva visheShaklR^ipteryukttaM mokShasya puruShArthatvamiti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "vikalpAmnAnAd.h' ityanena "tathA hi darshayati' ityanena cha "athAnandIhyevaiSha bhavati' ityAdishrutyA sukhamAtrAnubhavitvarUpavisheShasya klR^iptatvAditi vadatA sUchitaH |) || 8 || OM jagadvayApAravarjaM OM || ityatra, mukttAnAM satyasaN^kalpena jagatsR^iShyayAderIshvaradharmatvoktayA cha mukttAH kiM jagatsR^iShyayAdivyApArAnApnuvanti, na veti sandehe, ApnuvantIti pUrvaH pakShaH, neti siddhAntaH | tatra "samastakAryam.h' ityukttameva pUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati- 
nacha saN^kalpAdeva samastasambhavAtsR^iShyayAdisamastakAryasambhavaH vyApAro jagato viShNormukttAnAM tu svabhogagaH | nahi svaNarM shuddhamapi vahnikAryakaraM bhavet.h | ayogyashakttitastveva nAdhikAnandasambhavaH | 
|| nacha saN^kalpAdeveti || mukttasyeti sheShaH | satyasaN^kalpatvena kAmitasamastaprAptisambhavAtsR^iShyayAdisamastavyApArANAM mukttakAmyatvAtsR^iShyayAdisamastakAryasambhava ityarthaH | na chAprayojako hetuH | "sarvAnkAmAnAptvAmR^itaH samabhavatsamabhavaH' iti shruteH | sR^iShyayAdivyApArasya mukttakAmyatvAtkAmitAprAptau mukttasya satyakAmatvameva na syAditi bAdhakasatvAditi bhAvaH | evaMcha mukttAnAM satyasaN^kalpatvena jagatsR^iShyayAdisamastavyApAraprApteH na yukttaM lakShaNasUtramiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "jagadvayApAravarjam.h' iti pratiShedhena pratyakShopadeshAdityanena chashagatajagadvayApArAdyaishvaryANAM sarvadevatApUjyatvAdInAM samastAnAM kAryANAM cha saN^kalpAdeva sambhavatIti sUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "visheShaklR^iptiH' ityukttameva siddhAntanyAyaM pramANodAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- vyApAra iti || jagata iti sambandhe ShaShThI | sambandhashcha viShNorvyApAreNa jagato viShayaviShayibhAvaH | svabhogagaH svabhogaviShaya eveti sAvadhAraNam.h | vyApAra ityanuvartate | nanu mukttasyAj~nAnAdyapagamena shuddhatvAbhivyakttaj~nAnatvAdinA jagadvayApAraH kiM na syAdityata Aha- na hi svarNamiti || vahnikAryaM prakAshadAhAdikam.h | ayogyashakttita iti pUrvottarAbhyAM sambaddhayate ayogyashakttita eva tadyogyatArahitatvAdeva, natu pratibandhAdisadbhAvAdityarthaH | adhikAnandasambhavastviti tushabdasambandhaH | jagadvayApArasyApyupalakShaNam.h | ayogyakAryasya shaktayaviShayatve dR^iShyAntamAha- 
nahi kashchitsushaktto.api chakArAchetanaM chitim.h | nacha kAmastathA bhUyAttataH syAtsatyakAmiteti shrutyA visheShaklR^iptereva | mukttAnAM na jagadyatnastathApi vibudhAH sadA | mukttAnAM tu niyantArasteShAM brahmAsya vai haririti cha visheShaklR^iptiH || 9 || 
|| nahIti || chitiM chetanam.h, tarhi satyakAmatvahAniH syAdityata Aha- nacha kAmastviti || nanvasminnadhikaraNe 
"jagadvayApAravarjam.h' iti sUtreNa sR^iShyayAdivyApAravyatirikttasvAvaraniyAmakatvaM siddhAntatvenokttam.h, tatra sR^iShyayAdivyApAraprAptirUpasiddhAntAMshasyokttarItyA visheShaklR^iptyAlAbhe.api svAvaraniyAmakatvaprAptau kA yukttirityatastatrApi visheShaklR^iptimeva tAdR^ishapramANodAharaNapUrvakaM vivR^iNoti- mukttAnAmiti || yadyapIti sheShaH | evaMcha shrutyaiva visheShaklR^iptermukttasya jagadvayApArabhAvAdyukttaM lakShaNasUtramiti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH "AdhikArikamaNDalasthoktteH' ityanena "tathA hi darshayati' ityanena cheshvaragatajagadvayApAravyatirikttasvayogyakAmAnubhavitR^itvaM svAvaraniyAmakatvaM mahAchamasyashabdokttachaturmukhasyaiva sarvadevAbhipUjyatvamityevaMrUpasya visheShasya shrutiklR^iptasyaiva grAhyatvAditi vadatA sUchitaH |) || 9 || OM sthitimAha darshayatashchaivaM pratyakShAnumAne OM || ityatra, lokadarshanAlaukikatvAbhyAM muktta AnandAdivR^iddhihrAsavAnna veti sandehe, vR^iddhayAdimAniti pUrvaH pakShaH, neti siddhAntaH | tatra "vashitA' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradasharnapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati-
nacha vashitvAnmukttasyApi vR^iddhiH kR^itakR^ityatvena niHshramatvAdupAsanAdAvabhyAsapATavAnnirdoShatvAtsnehAdhikyAchcha tasyaiva paramasukharUpatvena phalarUpatvAt.h | 
||  nacha vashitvamiti || vR^iddhiH AnandAdeH, mukttasya vashitvAtkAmitAsheShaprApterAnandAdivR^iddheriShyatvenAkAmAnAnupapatteryukttA sukhAbhivR^iddhiriti bhAvaH | kiJNcha "etatsAma gAyannAste' ityAdinA mukttasyApyupAsanAshravaNAtsukhAdivR^iddhireShyavyA | anyathA tadvaiyarthyAditi | evaMcha vashitvena mukttasyApi vR^iddhayAdisadbhAvAtsaMsArasamAnadharmatvena muktterapuruShArthatvamiti neti bhAvaH | (ayaM cha nyAyaH "sthitimAha' ityanena yathAvasthita eva mukttastiShThati, na vR^iddhihrAsavAniti sUchanena sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena "kR^itanishramashcha' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivakShitAMshapUraNena vivR^iNoti- kR^itakR^ityatveneti || mukttasyeti sheShaH | ayaM bhAvaH | vashitvenApAdyamAnA vR^iddhiH kiM yogyasyotAyogyasya, nAdyaH, kR^itakR^ityatvena yogyasya prAptatvena niHshramatvAttadviShayakashramAbhAvAt.h | na dvitIyaH, kR^itakR^ityatvena mukttatvena "nachAyogyaM mukttigo.api prApnuyAnna cha kAmayet.h' iti mukttasyAyogyakAmanAniShedhena niHshramatvAdayogyaphalarAgAdidoSharahitatvAt.h | tathAcha vashitvamaprayojakamiti | anena anuvyAkhyAne kR^itashabdena kR^itakR^ityatvaM chashabdena upAsanAdAvabhyAsapATavAdityuchyata iti vivR^itaM bhavati | nanvevaM satyupAsanAdikAraNaM na syAdityatasyAnyathAsiddhipratipAdanaparatayApi kR^itaniHshrama ityukttanyAyaM vivR^iNoti- kR^itakR^ityatveneti || upAsanAdAvityatrApi sambaddhayate | kR^itetyataH pUrvaM mukttasyeti phalarUpatvAdityataH paraM tadupAsanaM na sAdhanamityapi pUraNIyam.h | kR^itakR^ityatvena mukttatvenopAsanAdiviShaye niHshramatvAchChramAdidoSharahitatvAdasAdhanarUpamapyupAsanAdi mukttena kriyata ityarthaH | atraiva samushchitayukttimAha- 
abhyAsapATavAtsnehAdashramatvAdupAsanA | bhakttishcha sukharUpaiva mukttAnAM na tu sAdhanamiti shrutiH || 10 || 
|| abhyAseti || tarhi saMsArakAlAbhyastaM niShiddhamapi kuryAdityata ukttam.h- nirdoShatvAditi || tathApyupAsanAderviShNuviShayatve kiM nimittamityata Aha- snehAdhikyAchcheti || viShNAviti sheShaH | evamapi niShprayojanamupAsanAdikaM kimarthaM kriyata ityata ukttam.h- tasyaivetyAdi || tatra pramANamAha- abhyAsapATavAditi || evaMcha kR^itaniHshramatvena mukttAnAM vR^iddhayAdyabhAvAdyukttaM mokShasya puruShArthatvamiti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyo.anumAnapadena vR^iddhayAdau kAraNAbhAvarUpAnumAnoktayA muktena svayogyasya prAptatvAtkR^itakR^ityatvena nirdoShatvAt.h phalarAgAdidoShasya kAraNAbhAvAdayogyaprAptyApi vR^iddhirneti sUchitaH |) || 10 || OM anAvR^ittiH shabdAdanAvR^ittiH shabdAt.h OM || ityatrobhayathApi sambhavAtkiM mukttaH punarAvartate, na veti sandehe, punarAvartata iti pUrvaH pakShaH, neti siddhAntaH | tatra "vishvasambhAvanA' ityukttapUrvapakShanyAyaM tatsAdhyapradarshanapUrvakaM vivR^iNvanpratikShipati-
nachAnantatvAtkAlasya trayodashI paJNchadashIvatkadAchitsamastasyApi sambhavAnmukttasyApi punarAvR^ittyAshaN^keti vAchyam.h | 
|| nachAnantatvAditi || anantatvAditi paJNchamI saptamyarthe | anantatve.apItyapishabdasambandhaH | idAnImaparidR^ishyamAnA mukttapunarAvR^ittiH kadA syAdityata ukttam.h- anantatvAtkAlasyeti || samastasyApIti | kAlasyetyanuvartate | samApteriti sheShaH | tatra dR^iShyAntamAha- trayodashIti || trayodashIpaJNchadashIti bhAvapradhAno nirdeshaH | ayamarthaH | yadyapi svargAdigatAnAM yugamanvantarAdivAsitvena punarAvR^ittisambhave.api mukttAnAM samastakAlavAsitvena na punarAvR^ittisambhavaH, tathApi bhAratayuddhe trayodashyA eva paJNchadashItvanirdeshAttatra tithitrayasya yugapatsamAptivadanantatve.api kAlasya samastasyApi kadAchidyugapatsamAptisambhavAnmukttasyApi punarAvR^ittyAshaN^kayeti | evaMcha vishvasya samastasya kAlasya samAptisambhAvanayA mukttasya punarAvR^ittyAshaN^keti na vAchyamiti bhAvaH | (ayaMcha nyAyaH "anAvR^ittiH' ityanena mukttAnAmAvR^ittyabhAvaM samarthayatA kAlasyAnantatvAdbhAratayuddhe trayodashyA paJNchadashItvasyAsambhAvitasya kadAchitsambhavAnmukttasyAvR^ittiriti sUchitaH |) taddhetutvena 
"mAhAtmyam.h' ityukttasiddhAntanyAyaM vivR^iNoti-
satyakAmatvAdimAhAtmyAt.h | asheShakAmasatyatvAnmukttAnAM na punarbhavaH | yasmAtsa kAmayedeva nityamAtmApunarbhavamiti cha shrutiH || 11 || 
|| satyakAmatvAditi || Adipadena sarvakAmAvAptiH | nanu satyakAmatvAdimAhAtmye.api mukttasya kuto na punarAvR^ittyAshaN^kayetyaprayojakatvashaN^kAparihArapUrvakamukttArthapratipAdakaM pramANamAha- asheSheti || asheShetyataH pUrvaM svayogyetyupaskartavyam.h | kAmAnAM satyatvaM nAma prAptavyArthamAtraviShayatvaniyamaH | mukttAnAmityasyobhayatrApi sambandhaH | nanu mukttAnAmasheShakAmasatyatve.api, apunarbhavakAmanAbhAvena punarbhavasambhavAdaprayojako heturityata ukttam.h- yasmAditi || sa mukttavargaH nityaM kAmayedeva, natu kadAchinna kamAyet.h | duHkhAsambhinnasvarUpasukhAnubhavasya shubharUpatvAt.h | nahi kashchichChubhAtpunarAvR^ittikAmo.astIti | yadukttaM samastasyApi kAlasya kadAchitsamAptisambhava iti | tadvayAhatatvAdupekShaNIyameveti na dUShitam.h | evaMcha mukttAnAM satyakAmatvAdimAhAtmyAtpunarAvR^ittyabhAvena yukttaM mokShasya puruShArthatvamiti bhAvaH || 11 || OM (*??*)idAnIM svakR^itagranthe tanmUlabhUtanyAyagrathanAtmakasUtrarUpamImAMsAshAstre.api shiShyANAM bahumAnAtishayotpAdanArthaM svakR^itagranthasyAnanyasAdhyatvarUpamata eva vyAkhyeyamImAMsAshAstrasya duravagAhyatvAdirUpaM mAhAtmyaM varNayan.h svagranthasya prayojanamAha-
ityanantamahAnyAyamImAMsApAravAridheH | uttarANAtyashaktayaiva vyAkulIkR^itachetasAm.h | mandAnAmupakArAya mahatAM chochChritatAtmanAm.h | tadvisheShaparij~nAnapradIptArkamachetasAm.h | visheShagADhe manasi nitarAmupakArakaH | nyAyaplavo mayAkAri saN^kShepAtpramitAkSharaiH | vistaro.apyayamevasyAttadvisheShAtivedinAm.h | vyAkhyAnuvyAkhyayoreva vistaro yadudIritaH || analpachetasAM puMsAmalaM vij~nAnasiddhaye | tannyAyoddharaNe shakttA api hyetena susthiram.h || nyAyAnugaM manaH kuryuriti saN^grahalAlasAH | ko nAmAsheShavidyorusAgaronmathanoddhR^itam.h || sAkShAdvidyAdhirAjena nyAyAmR^itamanuttamam.h | asheShato.adhigachCheta vandyo vR^indArako.api san.h || evaM sudurlabhe.apyaddhA mahAnyAyaparAmR^ite | kechanAdhikriyante.atra tatprasAdAnuraJNjitAH || brahmAdyA amR^ite yadvatsAgaronmathoddhR^ite | ahaM tu tatprAsAdaikamahAspadabaloddhataH || nyAyAmR^itArNavasimamavagAhya vibhajya cha | saMkShepavistarAbhyAM cha chakAra vyAkR^itiM kR^itim.h || 
|| ityanantetyAdinA || itishabdaH prakArArthaH | AdyArthashcha | ananatatvaM saN^khayA | mahattvaM vyAptyAdimatvena | nyAyapratipAdakamImAMsAvAridherapAratvaM duravagAhyatvaM, bahvarthatvena | ata evottAraNe vyAkhyAnAdirUpe.atyashakttiH | evakAreNa vyAkulIkR^itachetastvasya shabdadoShAdidasharnanimittakatvaM vyAvartayati | uttAraNe.atyashakttireva kuta ityata ukttam.h- mandAnAmiti || tarhi j~nAnyupAdeyatA na syAdityata Aha- mahatAmiti || ukttasamuchchayArthashchashabdaH | uchChritAtmanAM bahuviShayaj~nAnasAdhanamAnasAnAm.h | tena nyAyaplavena jAtena visheShaj~nAnena madhyAhnasUryasadR^ishachetasAm.h | manasi mImAMsApAravAridhau visheShagADhe sati | mahatAmityasyopakAraka ityanenApi sambandhaH | visheShaj~nAnahetutvAnnitarAmityukttam.h | nyAyaplavo nyAyamAlArUpaH | arthasaN^kShepasya bahvakSharairapi sambhavAtpramitAkSharairityukttam.h | pramitAkSharatvaM tvalpAkSharopetaikapadAdereva pUrvottarapakShanyAyapratipAdakatvamanekAdhikaraNasambandhinyAyapratipAdakatvaM  cha draShyavyam.h | nanu yadi nyAyamAlArUpagranthenaiva visheShaparij~nAnam.h | tarhi nyAyavivaraNaM vyarthamityAshaN^kaya pariharati vistaro.apItyAdinA api yadyapi | kathaM tadvisheShAtivedanamityata ukttam.h- vyAkhyeti || bhAShyAnuvyAkhyAnayoreva vistaro nyAyaprapaJNchanarUpo yasmAttasmAttAbhyAM visheShAtivedanamiti pUveNa sambandhaH | tathApyanalpachetasAM puMsAmalamatishayena visheShaj~nAnasiddhaye nyAyavivaraNarUpo vistaraH kR^ita iti sheShaH | anenAlpachetasAM vistarAbhAve j~nAnameva na syAditi tatkaraNasyAvashyakatvaM sUchitam.h | nanu yadi vyAkhyAnuvyAkhyayoreva vistara udIritastarhi tAbhyAmeva j~nAnasambhavAnnyAyamAlArUpasaN^graha eva vyartho dUre tadvivaraNamityata Aha- tannyAyeti || ye.alpachetasaH | na kevalaM sUchitanyAyoddharaNe.ashakttAH | kintu tayorvyAkhyAnuvyAkhyayorukttAnAM nyAyAnAmuddharaNe.apyashakttA ete manonyAyAnugaM na kuryuH | saN^kShepavistararUpagranthadvayena mano na nyAyAnugaM kuryuH | tathA ye.analpachetasaH tannyAyoddharaNe shakttA api saN^ghrahalAlasA etena manonyAyAnugaM susthiraM na kuryuH | etena susthiraM kuryuH | hi yasmAttasmAtsaN^grahavistararUpagranthadvayaM kR^itamityarthaH | nanu kvachittannyAyoddharaNe shakttastarhi tenaiva sUchitanyAyoddhAreNa saN^grahaH kartuM shakyata ityata Aha- ko nAmeti || asheShavidyA urUsAgarA iva | sAkShAnmukhyataH | nyAyAmR^itam.h | nyAyapratipAdakasUtrAtmakam.h | mokShahetutvAdamR^itatvam.h | antataH | asheShataH | svasaN^gR^ihItanyAyapratipAdakatvAdinA | 
anyathoktayabhAve | kaimutyadyotanArthaM vR^indArake.apItyukttam.h | evaM tarhi mImAMsAshAstraM niradhikArikaM syAdityata Aha- evamiti || addhAnishchayena, kechana brahmAdyA ityetadatrApi sambaddhayate | nanu yadi brahmAdyA evAdhikriyante tarhi svena kathaM saN^kShepavistarau kR^itAvityata Aha- ahaM tviti || anena svasya mukhyavAyvavatAratvarUpavisheShaM dyotayati | bhagavatprasAdarUpamukhyAshravaNabalenAbhivR^iddhaH | saN^kShepeNa kR^itanyAyaplavaM vistareNa vyAkR^itiM nyAyavivaraNaM chetyarthaH | nanu granthakaraNe vAkyArthaj~nAnakaraNapATavAdinA bhavitavyam.h | IshvaraprasAdasya tu kvopayoga ityato j~nAnAderIshvaraprasAdasAdhyatve.anvayavyatirekAvAha- 
tatprasAdamR^ite kasya shakttiH saMsArasAgare | magnasya chetanasya syAttatkR^itAnukR^itau kvachit.h || nityAnandAmR^itasyanditakaTAkShaidhitasya tu | kA nu shakttirbhavennaiva tataH ko.atrAtivismayaH || vidyAvidye sukhaM duHkhamashakttiH shakttireva cha | utpattisthitinAshAshcha visheShAshcha pare.akhilAH || chetanAchetanasyAsya samastas yadichChayA | sa mama svakR^itenaiva prIyatAM puruShottamaH || 
|| tatprasAdamiti || kAraNatAgrahe vyatirekasya prAdhAnyAdAdau tadukttiH | kA shakttinar bhavetsarvApi bhavedityarthaH | na kevalaM granthakaraNe shakttereva bhagavadadhInatvaM kintu sarvasyApIti vadannanena granthena bhagavatprItimAshAste || vidyetyAdinA || paro niyamanAdyAH | "na R^ita tvatkriyate' iti shruteriti bhAvaH | tadevopapAditam.h- vidyetyAdinA || viShNuj~nAnavatsvaj~nAnamapyadhikAriNAM mokShahetutvAtsvarUpapradarshanapUrvakaM svagranthapratipAdyamAha- 
yasya trINyuditAni vedavachane rUpANi divyAnalaM baT.htaddarshanamitthamevanihitaM devasya bhargo mahat.h | vAyo rAmavachonayaM prathamakaM pR^ikSho dvitIyaM vapurmadhvo yattu tR^itIyametadamunA granthaH kR^itaH keshave | namo.aja(bja)bhavabhUryakShapuraHsarasurAshraya | nArAyaNAraNaM mahyaM mApate preyasAM priya || 
|| iti shrImadbrahmasUtrAnuvyAkhyAnyAyavivaraNe chaturthAdhyAyasya chaturthaH pAdaH || 
|| shrImannyAyavivaraNaM sampUrNam.h || 
|| yasyeti || idaM padyaM TIkAkAraireva tatratatra vyAkhyAtam.h | devatAnamanena granthaH samApanIyo, natu svastavanenetyAshayenAha- nama iti || preyasAM sakAshAditi sheShaH | araNamityapi sambodhanam.h | araNaM bhaveti sheSho vA | sampUrNavij~nAnasukhAdiyuktto doShojkhitaH sarvasumAnameyaH | brahmAdisajjIvagatiH paresho nArAyaNaH prItiyuto mayi syAt.h | tatvaprakAshikAsaMstho mayAnugrahato hareH | sannyAyavivR^iterbhAvo bAlabodhArthamuddhR^itaH |
